### [75] [Generative Neural Video Compression via Video Diffusion Prior](https://arxiv.org/abs/2512.05016)
*Qi Mao,Hao Cheng,Tinghan Yang,Libiao Jin,Siwei Ma*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: GNVC-VD是首个基于DiT的生成式神经视频压缩框架，利用视频扩散先验统一时空潜在压缩和序列级生成优化，解决了传统感知编码的闪烁伪影问题。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有感知编码主要依赖预训练图像生成先验来恢复高频细节，但其逐帧特性缺乏时间建模，不可避免地导致感知闪烁伪影。需要视频原生生成先验来确保时空一致性。

Method: 提出统一流匹配潜在优化模块，利用视频扩散变换器通过序列级去噪联合增强帧内和帧间潜在表示；从解码的时空潜在初始化优化而非纯高斯噪声；学习适应压缩退化的校正项；条件适配器向中间DiT层注入压缩感知线索。

Result: GNVC-VD在感知质量上超越传统和学习的编解码器，显著减少先前生成方法中持续的闪烁伪影，即使在0.01 bpp以下的极低比特率下也能保持良好性能。

Conclusion: 将视频原生生成先验集成到神经编解码器中，为下一代感知视频压缩提供了有前景的方向，解决了时间一致性问题并提升了极低比特率下的视觉质量。

Abstract: We present GNVC-VD, the first DiT-based generative neural video compression framework built upon an advanced video generation foundation model, where spatio-temporal latent compression and sequence-level generative refinement are unified within a single codec. Existing perceptual codecs primarily rely on pre-trained image generative priors to restore high-frequency details, but their frame-wise nature lacks temporal modeling and inevitably leads to perceptual flickering. To address this, GNVC-VD introduces a unified flow-matching latent refinement module that leverages a video diffusion transformer to jointly enhance intra- and inter-frame latents through sequence-level denoising, ensuring consistent spatio-temporal details. Instead of denoising from pure Gaussian noise as in video generation, GNVC-VD initializes refinement from decoded spatio-temporal latents and learns a correction term that adapts the diffusion prior to compression-induced degradation. A conditioning adaptor further injects compression-aware cues into intermediate DiT layers, enabling effective artifact removal while maintaining temporal coherence under extreme bitrate constraints. Extensive experiments show that GNVC-VD surpasses both traditional and learned codecs in perceptual quality and significantly reduces the flickering artifacts that persist in prior generative approaches, even below 0.01 bpp, highlighting the promise of integrating video-native generative priors into neural codecs for next-generation perceptual video compression.

中文标题: 基于视频扩散先验的生成式神经视频压缩

中文摘要: 我们提出了GNVC-VD，这是首个基于DiT的生成式神经视频压缩框架，建立在先进的视频生成基础模型之上，其中时空潜在压缩和序列级生成优化在单个编解码器中统一。现有感知编解码器主要依赖预训练图像生成先验来恢复高频细节，但其逐帧特性缺乏时间建模，不可避免地导致感知闪烁。为解决此问题，GNVC-VD引入了统一的流匹配潜在优化模块，利用视频扩散变换器通过序列级去噪联合增强帧内和帧间潜在表示，确保一致的时空细节。与视频生成中从纯高斯噪声去噪不同，GNVC-VD从解码的时空潜在初始化优化，并学习一个校正项来适应扩散先验到压缩引起的退化。条件适配器进一步将压缩感知线索注入中间DiT层，在极端比特率约束下实现有效的伪影去除同时保持时间一致性。大量实验表明，GNVC-VD在感知质量上超越传统和学习编解码器，并显著减少先前生成方法中持续的闪烁伪影，即使在0.01 bpp以下，突显了将视频原生生成先验集成到神经编解码器中用于下一代感知视频压缩的前景。

</details>


### [76] [RAMEN: Resolution-Adjustable Multimodal Encoder for Earth Observation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2512.05025)
*Nicolas Houdré,Diego Marcos,Hugo Riffaud de Turckheim,Dino Ienco,Laurent Wendling,Camille Kurtz,Sylvain Lobry*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: RAMEN是一个分辨率可调的多模态地球观测编码器，能够处理不同传感器、分辨率的EO数据，通过将空间分辨率作为可控输出参数，让用户可以在推理时直接控制细节级别，在空间精度和计算成本之间进行权衡。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 地球观测数据具有广泛的空间、光谱和时间分辨率差异，现有基础模型通常需要固定输入分辨率或基于特定传感器编码器，限制了在异构EO模态间的泛化能力。需要一种传感器无关的统一编码器来处理不同分辨率的EO数据。

Method: RAMEN将模态、空间和时间分辨率作为关键输入特征，通过统一的transformer编码器重建来自不同来源的掩码多模态EO数据。核心方法是将空间分辨率定义为可控输出参数，使用户能在推理时直接控制所需细节级别。

Result: RAMEN在社区标准PANGAEA基准测试中表现出色，包含各种多传感器和多分辨率下游任务，超越了更大的最先进模型。模型能够有效迁移到已知和未见过的传感器配置。

Conclusion: RAMEN提供了一种传感器无关的统一编码器，能够处理不同分辨率的EO数据，通过将分辨率作为可控参数，实现了空间精度和计算成本之间的灵活权衡，在多个下游任务中表现出优越性能。

Abstract: Earth observation (EO) data spans a wide range of spatial, spectral, and temporal resolutions, from high-resolution optical imagery to low resolution multispectral products or radar time series. While recent foundation models have improved multimodal integration for learning meaningful representations, they often expect fixed input resolutions or are based on sensor-specific encoders limiting generalization across heterogeneous EO modalities. To overcome these limitations we introduce RAMEN, a resolution-adjustable multimodal encoder that learns a shared visual representation across EO data in a fully sensor-agnostic manner. RAMEN treats the modality and spatial and temporal resolutions as key input data features, enabling coherent analysis across modalities within a unified latent space. Its main methodological contribution is to define spatial resolution as a controllable output parameter, giving users direct control over the desired level of detail at inference and allowing explicit trade-offs between spatial precision and computational cost. We train a single, unified transformer encoder reconstructing masked multimodal EO data drawn from diverse sources, ensuring generalization across sensors and resolutions. Once pretrained, RAMEN transfers effectively to both known and unseen sensor configurations and outperforms larger state-of-the-art models on the community-standard PANGAEA benchmark, containing various multi-sensor and multi-resolution downstream tasks. Our code and pretrained model are available at https://github.com/nicolashoudre/RAMEN.

中文标题: RAMEN：分辨率可调的地球观测多模态编码器

中文摘要: 地球观测数据涵盖了广泛的空间、光谱和时间分辨率，从高分辨率光学图像到低分辨率多光谱产品或雷达时间序列。虽然最近的基础模型改进了多模态集成以学习有意义的表示，但它们通常期望固定的输入分辨率或基于特定传感器的编码器，限制了在异构EO模态间的泛化能力。为了克服这些限制，我们引入了RAMEN，一种分辨率可调的多模态编码器，以完全传感器无关的方式学习EO数据的共享视觉表示。RAMEN将模态、空间和时间分辨率作为关键输入数据特征，在统一的潜在空间内实现跨模态的连贯分析。其主要方法贡献是将空间分辨率定义为可控输出参数，让用户在推理时直接控制所需细节级别，并允许在空间精度和计算成本之间进行明确的权衡。我们训练了一个统一的transformer编码器，重建来自不同来源的掩码多模态EO数据，确保跨传感器和分辨率的泛化能力。一旦预训练完成，RAMEN能够有效迁移到已知和未见过的传感器配置，并在社区标准PANGAEA基准测试中超越了更大的最先进模型，该基准包含各种多传感器和多分辨率的下游任务。我们的代码和预训练模型可在https://github.com/nicolashoudre/RAMEN获取。

This process gives clear insights into the facial structure before we move on to creating detailed images. In the first stage, we blend two techniques: one that focuses on local features with CNNs and global features with Vision Transformers. This helped us create clear and detailed semantic layouts. The architecture naturally handles arbitrary mask configurations through dynamic attention without maskspecific training. ### [78] [4DLangVGGT: 4D Language-Visual Geometry Grounded Transformer](https://arxiv.org/abs/2512.05060)
*Xianfeng Wu,Yajing Bai,Minghan Li,Xianzu Wu,Xueqi Zhao,Zhongyuan Lai,Wenyu Liu,Xinggang Wang*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 4DLangVGGT是首个基于Transformer的前馈统一框架，用于4D语言基础，通过联合几何感知和语言对齐实现高效部署和强泛化能力，在多个数据集上达到SOTA性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 构建4D语言场对于具身AI、AR/VR和4D场景理解至关重要，但现有方法依赖场景特定的高斯泼溅技术，存在逐场景优化成本高、泛化能力有限、难以扩展到实际应用等问题。

Method: 提出4DLangVGGT框架，包含两个关键组件：1) StreamVGGT（4D视觉几何Transformer）捕捉动态场景的时空几何表示；2) SBD（语义桥接解码器）将几何感知特征投影到语言对齐的语义空间。

Result: 在HyperNeRF和Neu3D数据集上，4DLangVGGT不仅有效泛化，而且达到最先进性能：逐场景训练下提升高达2%，多场景训练下提升1%。

Conclusion: 4DLangVGGT通过统一的Transformer架构解决了现有方法的局限性，实现了高效部署和强泛化能力，为开放词汇4D场景理解建立了新范式，具有大规模部署的实用性。

Abstract: Constructing 4D language fields is crucial for embodied AI, augmented/virtual reality, and 4D scene understanding, as they provide enriched semantic representations of dynamic environments and enable open-vocabulary querying in complex scenarios. However, existing approaches to 4D semantic field construction primarily rely on scene-specific Gaussian splatting, which requires per-scene optimization, exhibits limited generalization, and is difficult to scale to real-world applications. To address these limitations, we propose 4DLangVGGT, the first Transformer-based feed-forward unified framework for 4D language grounding, that jointly integrates geometric perception and language alignment within a single architecture. 4DLangVGGT has two key components: the 4D Visual Geometry Transformer, StreamVGGT, which captures spatio-temporal geometric representations of dynamic scenes; and the Semantic Bridging Decoder (SBD), which projects geometry-aware features into a language-aligned semantic space, thereby enhancing semantic interpretability while preserving structural fidelity. Unlike prior methods that depend on costly per-scene optimization, 4DLangVGGT can be jointly trained across multiple dynamic scenes and directly applied during inference, achieving both deployment efficiency and strong generalization. This design significantly improves the practicality of large-scale deployment and establishes a new paradigm for open-vocabulary 4D scene understanding. Experiments on HyperNeRF and Neu3D datasets demonstrate that our approach not only generalizes effectively but also achieves state-of-the-art performance, achieving up to 2% gains under per-scene training and 1% improvements under multi-scene training. ### [79] [BulletTime: Decoupled Control of Time and Camera Pose for Video Generation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2512.05076)

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 提出4D可控视频扩散框架，将连续世界时间序列和相机轨迹作为条件输入，通过注意力层的4D位置编码和特征调制的自适应归一化注入到视频扩散模型中。创建了时间与相机变化独立参数化的独特数据集。

Abstract: Emerging video diffusion models achieve high visual fidelity but fundamentally couple scene dynamics with camera motion, limiting their ability to provide precise spatial and temporal control. We introduce a 4D-controllable video diffusion framework that explicitly decouples scene dynamics from camera pose, enabling fine-grained manipulation of both scene dynamics and camera viewpoint. Our framework takes continuous world-time sequences and camera trajectories as conditioning inputs, injecting them into the video diffusion model through a 4D positional encoding in the attention layer and adaptive normalizations for feature modulation. To train this model, we curate a unique dataset in which temporal and camera variations are independently parameterized; this dataset will be made public. ### [80] [Deep Forcing: Training-Free Long Video Generation with Deep Sink and Participative Compression](https://arxiv.org/abs/2512.05081)
*Jung Yi,Wooseok Jang,Paul Hyunbin Cho,Jisu Nam,Heeji Yoon,Seungryong Kim*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: Deep Forcing是一种无需训练的长视频生成方法，通过Deep Sink和Participative Compression两种机制解决现有视频扩散模型中的时间重复、漂移和运动减速问题，实现12倍以上的外推生成（如从5秒训练扩展到60秒以上生成）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的自回归视频扩散方法虽然实现了实时帧流式生成，但仍存在时间重复、漂移和运动减速等问题。直接将StreamingLLM风格的注意力sink应用于视频扩散会导致保真度下降和运动停滞，因此需要一种无需微调的解决方案。

Method: Deep Forcing包含两种无需训练的机制：1) Deep Sink：将滑动窗口的一半分配给持久sink token，并重新对齐其时间RoPE相位到当前时间线，在长序列生成中稳定全局上下文；2) Participative Compression：执行重要性感知的KV缓存剪枝，仅保留最近注意力中活跃参与的token，安全丢弃冗余和退化的历史信息，最小化分布外长度生成时的误差累积。

Result: 该方法实现了超过12倍的外推生成（如从5秒训练扩展到60秒以上），在图像质量上优于LongLive，在美学质量上优于RollingForcing，几乎保持整体一致性，并在动态程度上获得显著提升，同时保持实时生成能力。

Conclusion: Deep Forcing证明无需训练的KV缓存管理方法在自回归流式长视频生成任务中能够匹配甚至超越基于训练的方法，为长视频生成提供了一种高效且无需额外训练的解决方案。

Abstract: Recent advances in autoregressive video diffusion have enabled real-time frame streaming, yet existing solutions still suffer from temporal repetition, drift, and motion deceleration. We find that naively applying StreamingLLM-style attention sinks to video diffusion leads to fidelity degradation and motion stagnation. To overcome this, we introduce Deep Forcing, which consists of two training-free mechanisms that address this without any fine-tuning. Specifically, 1) Deep Sink dedicates half of the sliding window to persistent sink tokens and re-aligns their temporal RoPE phase to the current timeline, stabilizing global context during long rollouts. 2) Participative Compression performs importance-aware KV cache pruning that preserves only tokens actively participating in recent attention while safely discarding redundant and degraded history, minimizing error accumulation under out-of-distribution length generation. Together, these components enable over 12x extrapolation (e.g. 5s-trained to 60s+ generation) with better imaging quality than LongLive, better aesthetic quality than RollingForcing, almost maintaining overall consistency, and substantial gains in dynamic degree, all while maintaining real-time generation. Our results demonstrate that training-free KV-cache management can match or exceed training-based approaches for autoregressively streaming long-video generation.

中文标题: 深度强制：基于深度汇聚和参与式压缩的无训练长视频生成

中文摘要: 自回归视频扩散的最新进展实现了实时帧流式生成，但现有解决方案仍存在时间重复、漂移和运动减速问题。我们发现，将StreamingLLM风格的注意力汇聚直接应用于视频扩散会导致保真度下降和运动停滞。为克服这一问题，我们提出了Deep Forcing，包含两种无需训练的机制：1) Deep Sink将滑动窗口的一半分配给持久汇聚token，并重新对齐其时间RoPE相位到当前时间线，在长序列生成中稳定全局上下文；2) Participative Compression执行重要性感知的KV缓存剪枝，仅保留最近注意力中活跃参与的token，安全丢弃冗余和退化的历史信息，最小化分布外长度生成时的误差累积。这些组件共同实现了超过12倍的外推生成（如从5秒训练扩展到60秒以上），在图像质量上优于LongLive，在美学质量上优于RollingForcing，几乎保持整体一致性，并在动态程度上获得显著提升，同时保持实时生成。我们的结果表明，无需训练的KV缓存管理方法在自回归流式长视频生成任务中能够匹配甚至超越基于训练的方法。

### [81] [Visual Reasoning Tracer: Object-Level Grounded Reasoning Benchmark](https://arxiv.org/abs/2512.05091)
*Haobo Yuan,Yueyi Sun,Yanwei Li,Tao Zhang,Xueqing Deng,Henghui Ding,Lu Qi,Anran Wang,Xiangtai Li,Ming-Hsuan Yang*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 本文提出了视觉推理追踪器（VRT）任务，要求模型不仅定位目标对象，还要显式预测构成推理路径的中间对象，以解决当前多模态大语言模型推理过程不透明的问题。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前多模态大语言模型在视觉定位和视觉问答等任务上取得了显著进展，但模型的推理过程仍然不透明——通常只输出最终预测，而不揭示导致结果的中间步骤或细粒度证据（如像素、位置）。这与人类智能通过视觉推理链自然运作的方式形成对比。

Method: 作者提出了视觉推理追踪器（VRT）任务，并贡献了三个核心组件：1）VRT-Bench：用于评估视觉推理的人工标注基准；2）评估推理轨迹质量的新指标；3）VRT-80k：用于推理模型训练的大规模数据集。

Result: 实验表明，现有模型虽然经常能产生正确的最终输出，但在中间推理的定位方面表现不佳。相比之下，在VRT-80k数据集上训练的模型在追踪推理路径方面取得了显著改进。

Conclusion: VRT任务和配套的数据集、基准及指标为解决多模态大语言模型推理过程不透明的问题提供了有效途径，推动了视觉推理可解释性的研究。

Abstract: Recent advances in Multimodal Large Language Models (MLLMs) have significantly improved performance on tasks such as visual grounding and visual question answering. However, the reasoning processes of these models remain largely opaque; they typically output only final predictions without revealing the intermediate steps or fine-grained evidence (e.g., pixels, locations) that lead to the result. This contrasts with human intelligence, which naturally operates through a chain of visual reasoning. To address this limitation, we introduce the Visual Reasoning Tracer (VRT) task, which requires models to not only localize the target object but also explicitly predict the intermediate objects that form the reasoning path. To advance research in this area, we contribute: (1) VRT-Bench, a human-annotated benchmark for evaluating visual reasoning; (2) a new metric for assessing the quality of reasoning traces; and (3) VRT-80k, a large-scale dataset for reasoning model training. Our experiments reveal that while existing models often produce the correct final output, they struggle to ground their intermediate reasoning. In contrast, models trained on VRT-80k achieve substantial improvements in tracing the reasoning path.

中文标题: 视觉推理追踪器：对象级基础推理基准

Method: 1. 提出空间美学评估范式，包含布局、和谐、照明、失真四个维度；2. 构建SA-BENCH基准数据集（18,000张图像，50,000个标注）；3. 通过MLLM微调和多维融合方法开发SA-IQA框架；4. 应用于GRPO强化学习和Best-of-N选择两个下游任务。

### [83] [EvoIR: Towards All-in-One Image Restoration via Evolutionary Frequency Modulation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2512.05104)
*Jiaqi Ma,Shengkai Hu,Jun Wan,Jiaxing Huang,Lefei Zhang,Salman Khan*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: EvoIR是一个面向"一体化图像恢复"的框架，通过进化频率调制动态适应多种退化类型，在多个基准测试中优于现有方法。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的一体化图像恢复方法通常缺乏显式的频率建模，依赖固定或启发式的优化策略，限制了在异质退化类型上的泛化能力。

Method: 提出EvoIR框架：1) 频率调制模块(FMM)显式地将特征分解为高低频分支并自适应调制；2) 进化优化策略(EOS)通过基于种群的进化过程迭代调整频率感知目标，动态平衡结构精度和感知保真度。

Result: 在多个基准测试上的广泛实验表明，EvoIR优于最先进的一体化图像恢复方法，FMM和EOS的协同作用比单独使用任一组件带来更大改进。

Conclusion: EvoIR通过进化频率调制为一体化图像恢复提供了动态自适应解决方案，显式频率建模和进化优化的结合有效解决了异质退化类型的挑战。

Abstract: All-in-One Image Restoration (AiOIR) tasks often involve diverse degradation that require robust and versatile strategies. However, most existing approaches typically lack explicit frequency modeling and rely on fixed or heuristic optimization schedules, which limit the generalization across heterogeneous degradation. To address these limitations, we propose EvoIR, an AiOIR-specific framework that introduces evolutionary frequency modulation for dynamic and adaptive image restoration. Specifically, EvoIR employs the Frequency-Modulated Module (FMM) that decomposes features into high- and low-frequency branches in an explicit manner and adaptively modulates them to enhance both structural fidelity and fine-grained details. Central to EvoIR, an Evolutionary Optimization Strategy (EOS) iteratively adjusts frequency-aware objectives through a population-based evolutionary process, dynamically balancing structural accuracy and perceptual fidelity. Its evolutionary guidance further mitigates gradient conflicts across degradation and accelerates convergence. By synergizing FMM and EOS, EvoIR yields greater improvements than using either component alone, underscoring their complementary roles. Extensive experiments on multiple benchmarks demonstrate that EvoIR outperforms state-of-the-art AiOIR methods.

中文标题: EvoIR：通过进化频率调制实现一体化图像恢复

中文摘要: 一体化图像恢复任务通常涉及多种退化类型，需要鲁棒且通用的策略。然而，大多数现有方法通常缺乏显式的频率建模，并依赖固定或启发式的优化策略，这限制了在异质退化类型上的泛化能力。为解决这些限制，我们提出了EvoIR，一个针对一体化图像恢复的框架，引入了进化频率调制以实现动态自适应的图像恢复。具体来说，EvoIR采用频率调制模块，以显式方式将特征分解为高频和低频分支，并自适应地调制它们以增强结构保真度和细粒度细节。EvoIR的核心是进化优化策略，通过基于种群的进化过程迭代调整频率感知目标，动态平衡结构精度和感知保真度。其进化指导进一步缓解了跨退化的梯度冲突并加速收敛。通过协同FMM和EOS，EvoIR比单独使用任一组件带来更大改进，强调了它们的互补作用。在多个基准测试上的广泛实验表明，EvoIR优于最先进的一体化图像恢复方法。

### [85] [ARM-Thinker: Reinforcing Multimodal Generative Reward Models with Agentic Tool Use and Visual Reasoning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2512.05111)

Method: 提出ARM-Thinker，一种智能多模态奖励模型，通过自主调用外部工具来验证判断证据。采用多阶段强化学习联合优化工具调用决策和判断准确性，并引入ARMBench-VL评估框架。

Result: ARM-Thinker在奖励建模基准上平均提升16.2%，在工具使用任务上提升9.6%，在多模态数学和逻辑推理基准上优于基线模型，显著提升了准确性和可解释性。

This enables the model to verify fine-grained visual details, cross-reference multi-page evidence, and validate reasoning claims, which are capabilities absent in existing reward models. ### [86] [DraCo: Draft as CoT for Text-to-Image Preview and Rare Concept Generation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2512.05112)
*Dongzhi Jiang,Renrui Zhang,Haodong Li,Zhuofan Zong,Ziyu Guo,Jun He,Claire Guo,Junyan Ye,Rongyao Fang,Weijia Li,Rui Liu,Hongsheng Li*

TL;DR: DraCo提出了一种新颖的文本到图像生成方法，通过生成低分辨率草稿图像作为视觉思维链，然后进行语义验证和选择性校正，解决了文本规划粗粒度和罕见概念生成的难题。

Method: DraCo采用交错推理范式：1）首先生成低分辨率草稿图像作为视觉预览；2）利用模型理解能力验证草稿与文本提示的语义对齐；3）通过选择性校正和超分辨率进行细化。还提出了DraCo-240K训练数据集和DraCo-CFG引导策略。

Result: 在多个基准测试中取得显著提升：GenEval提升8%，Imagine-Bench提升0.91分，GenEval++提升3%。显著优于直接生成和其他基于思维链的生成方法，特别是在罕见概念生成方面表现突出。

Conclusion: DraCo通过将视觉草稿作为思维链的中间表示，有效解决了文本到图像生成中的规划粗粒度和罕见概念生成难题。该方法展示了交错推理在视觉生成任务中的潜力，为多模态生成提供了新的研究方向。

Abstract: Recent unified multimodal large language models (MLLMs) have shown impressive capabilities, incorporating chain-of-thought (CoT) reasoning for enhanced text-to-image generation. However, existing approaches remain limited, either treating the model merely as a standalone generator or relying on abstract textual planning. To this end, we propose Draft-as-CoT (DraCo), a novel interleaved reasoning paradigm that fully leverages both textual and visual contents in CoT for better planning and verification. Our method first generates a low-resolution draft image as preview, providing more concrete and structural visual planning and guidance. Then, we employ the model's inherent understanding capability to verify potential semantic misalignments between the draft and input prompt, and performs refinement through selective corrections with super-resolution. In this way, our approach addresses two fundamental challenges: the coarse-grained nature of textual planning and the difficulty in generating rare attribute combinations. To support training, we curate DraCo-240K, aiming to enhance three atomic capabilities spanning general correction, instance manipulation, and layout reorganization. Supported by DraCo-CFG, a specialized classifier-free guidance (CFG) strategy for interleaved reasoning, DraCo achieves a tremendous increase on GenEval (+8%), Imagine-Bench (+0.91), and GenEval++ (+3%), significantly outperforming direct generation and other generation methods empowered by CoT.

中文标题: DraCo：以草稿作为思维链的文本到图像预览与罕见概念生成

中文摘要: 最近统一的多模态大语言模型（MLLMs）展现出令人印象深刻的能力，通过思维链（CoT）推理增强了文本到图像的生成。然而，现有方法仍然有限，要么将模型仅视为独立的生成器，要么依赖于抽象的文本规划。为此，我们提出了草稿作为思维链（DraCo），这是一种新颖的交错推理范式，充分利用思维链中的文本和视觉内容进行更好的规划和验证。我们的方法首先生成低分辨率草稿图像作为预览，提供更具体和结构化的视觉规划和指导。然后，我们利用模型固有的理解能力来验证草稿与输入提示之间潜在语义不匹配，并通过选择性校正和超分辨率进行细化。通过这种方式，我们的方法解决了两个基本挑战：文本规划的粗粒度性质以及生成罕见属性组合的困难。为了支持训练，我们策划了DraCo-240K数据集，旨在增强三个原子能力：通用校正、实例操作和布局重组。在DraCo-CFG的支持下，这是一种专门用于交错推理的分类器自由引导策略，DraCo在GenEval（+8%）、Imagine-Bench（+0.91）和GenEval++（+3%）上实现了巨大提升，显著优于直接生成和其他由思维链增强的生成方法。

</details>


### [87] [Splannequin: Freezing Monocular Mannequin-Challenge Footage with Dual-Detection Splatting](https://arxiv.org/abs/2512.05113)
*Hao-Jen Chien,Yi-Chuan Huang,Chung-Ho Wu,Wei-Lun Chao,Yu-Lun Liu*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: Splannequin提出了一种用于从单目人体模型挑战视频中合成高质量冻结3D场景的方法，通过检测高斯原语中的隐藏和缺陷状态，并应用时间锚定来解决动态高斯溅射中的伪影问题。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 从单目人体模型挑战视频中合成高保真冻结3D场景是一个独特问题，不同于标准的动态场景重建。目标是在创建冻结场景的同时，战略性地保留细微动态以实现用户控制的即时选择。现有方法在单目捕获和稀疏时间监督下会产生重影和模糊等伪影。

Method: 提出Splannequin方法，这是一种架构无关的正则化技术，检测高斯原语中的两种状态：隐藏状态和缺陷状态，并应用时间锚定。在主要前向相机运动下，隐藏状态锚定到最近观察良好的过去状态，而缺陷状态锚定到具有更强监督的未来状态。该方法通过简单的损失项集成到现有动态高斯管道中，无需架构更改，且不增加推理开销。

Result: 该方法显著提高了视觉质量，实现了高保真、用户可选择的冻结时间渲染，在用户偏好测试中获得了96%的偏好率。

Conclusion: Splannequin通过检测和锚定高斯原语中的隐藏和缺陷状态，有效解决了单目人体模型挑战视频中冻结场景合成的伪影问题，提供了一种简单有效的方法来提升动态高斯溅射在特定应用场景中的性能。

Abstract: Synthesizing high-fidelity frozen 3D scenes from monocular Mannequin-Challenge (MC) videos is a unique problem distinct from standard dynamic scene reconstruction. Instead of focusing on modeling motion, our goal is to create a frozen scene while strategically preserving subtle dynamics to enable user-controlled instant selection. To achieve this, we introduce a novel application of dynamic Gaussian splatting: the scene is modeled dynamically, which retains nearby temporal variation, and a static scene is rendered by fixing the model's time parameter. However, under this usage, monocular capture with sparse temporal supervision introduces artifacts like ghosting and blur for Gaussians that become unobserved or occluded at weakly supervised timestamps. We propose Splannequin, an architecture-agnostic regularization that detects two states of Gaussian primitives, hidden and defective, and applies temporal anchoring. Under predominantly forward camera motion, hidden states are anchored to their recent well-observed past states, while defective states are anchored to future states with stronger supervision. Our method integrates into existing dynamic Gaussian pipelines via simple loss terms, requires no architectural changes, and adds zero inference overhead. This results in markedly improved visual quality, enabling high-fidelity, user-selectable frozen-time renderings, validated by a 96% user preference. Project page: https://chien90190.github.io/splannequin/

中文标题: Splannequin：通过双重检测溅射冻结单目人体模型挑战视频

中文摘要: 从单目人体模型挑战视频中合成高保真冻结3D场景是一个独特问题，不同于标准的动态场景重建。我们的目标不是专注于建模运动，而是创建冻结场景，同时战略性地保留细微动态以实现用户控制的即时选择。为实现这一目标，我们引入了动态高斯溅射的新颖应用：场景被动态建模以保留附近的时间变化，并通过固定模型的时间参数来渲染静态场景。然而，在这种使用方式下，单目捕获和稀疏时间监督会引入伪影，如对于在弱监督时间戳变得不可见或被遮挡的高斯原语产生重影和模糊。我们提出了Splannequin，这是一种架构无关的正则化方法，检测高斯原语的两种状态：隐藏和缺陷状态，并应用时间锚定。在主要前向相机运动下，隐藏状态锚定到其最近观察良好的过去状态，而缺陷状态锚定到具有更强监督的未来状态。我们的方法通过简单的损失项集成到现有动态高斯管道中，无需架构更改，且不增加推理开销。这显著提高了视觉质量，实现了高保真、用户可选择的冻结时间渲染，在用户偏好测试中获得了96%的偏好率。

### [88] [Light-X: Generative 4D Video Rendering with Camera and Illumination Control](https://arxiv.org/abs/2512.05115)
*Tianqi Liu,Zhaoxi Chen,Zihao Huang,Shaocong Xu,Saining Zhang,Chongjie Ye,Bohan Li,Zhiguo Cao,Wei Li,Hao Zhao,Ziwei Liu*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: Light-X是一个生成式4D视频渲染框架，能够从单目视频中实现相机轨迹和照明的联合控制，通过解耦几何与光照信号实现高质量渲染。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有光照控制方法在视频应用中面临光照保真度与时间一致性的权衡问题。真实场景的生成建模需要相机轨迹和照明的联合控制，因为视觉动态本质上由几何和光照共同塑造。

Method: 1) 提出解耦设计：通过动态点云沿用户定义相机轨迹投影捕捉几何和运动，通过重照明帧投影到相同几何提供光照线索；2) 引入Light-Syn合成训练数据：通过基于退化的逆映射管道从野外单目视频合成多视角多光照训练对。

Result: Light-X在联合相机-光照控制方面优于基线方法，在文本条件和背景条件设置下均超越先前的视频重照明方法。

Conclusion: Light-X通过解耦几何与光照信号，结合合成训练数据策略，实现了从单目视频中高质量、可控的4D视频渲染，推进了真实场景生成建模的发展。

Abstract: Recent advances in illumination control extend image-based methods to video, yet still facing a trade-off between lighting fidelity and temporal consistency. Moving beyond relighting, a key step toward generative modeling of real-world scenes is the joint control of camera trajectory and illumination, since visual dynamics are inherently shaped by both geometry and lighting. To this end, we present Light-X, a video generation framework that enables controllable rendering from monocular videos with both viewpoint and illumination control. 1) We propose a disentangled design that decouples geometry and lighting signals: geometry and motion are captured via dynamic point clouds projected along user-defined camera trajectories, while illumination cues are provided by a relit frame consistently projected into the same geometry. These explicit, fine-grained cues enable effective disentanglement and guide high-quality illumination. 2) To address the lack of paired multi-view and multi-illumination videos, we introduce Light-Syn, a degradation-based pipeline with inverse-mapping that synthesizes training pairs from in-the-wild monocular footage. This strategy yields a dataset covering static, dynamic, and AI-generated scenes, ensuring robust training. Extensive experiments show that Light-X outperforms baseline methods in joint camera-illumination control and surpasses prior video relighting methods under both text- and background-conditioned settings.

中文标题: Light-X：具有相机和光照控制的生成式4D视频渲染

中文摘要: 最近的光照控制进展将基于图像的方法扩展到视频领域，但仍面临光照保真度与时间一致性的权衡。超越重照明，实现真实场景生成建模的关键步骤是相机轨迹和照明的联合控制，因为视觉动态本质上由几何和光照共同塑造。为此，我们提出了Light-X，一个视频生成框架，能够从单目视频中实现视角和光照的可控渲染。1) 我们提出了一种解耦设计，将几何和光照信号分离：几何和运动通过沿用户定义相机轨迹投影的动态点云捕捉，而光照线索由重照明帧一致投影到相同几何提供。这些明确、细粒度的线索实现了有效的解耦并指导高质量光照。2) 为了解决缺乏配对多视角和多光照视频的问题，我们引入了Light-Syn，一个基于退化的逆映射管道，从野外单目视频合成训练对。该策略产生了一个涵盖静态、动态和AI生成场景的数据集，确保了鲁棒的训练。大量实验表明，Light-X在联合相机-光照控制方面优于基线方法，在文本条件和背景条件设置下均超越先前的视频重照明方法。

### [89] [CRAFT-E: A Neuro-Symbolic Framework for Embodied Affordance Grounding](https://arxiv.org/abs/2512.04231)
*Zhou Chen,Joe Lin,Carson Bulgin,Sathyanarayanan N. Aakur*

Main category: cs.RO

TL;DR: CRAFT-E是一个神经符号框架，通过结合知识图谱、视觉语言对齐和抓取推理，实现可解释的具身可供性接地，用于辅助机器人选择合适的功能性物体。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 辅助机器人在非结构化环境中需要理解物体的功能用途，而现有方法多为黑盒模型或固定标签，缺乏透明度、可控性和可靠性，难以满足面向人类应用的需求。

Method: 采用模块化神经符号框架，结合结构化动词-属性-对象知识图谱、视觉语言对齐和基于能量的抓取推理，生成可解释的接地路径，将抓取可行性纳入可供性推理。

Result: 在静态场景、ImageNet功能检索和真实世界试验（20个动词、39个物体）中表现优异，框架在感知噪声下保持鲁棒性，提供透明诊断，并在物理机器人上成功部署。

Conclusion: CRAFT-E通过耦合符号推理与具身感知，为可供性接地的对象选择提供了可解释、可定制的替代方案，支持辅助机器人系统中的可信决策，优于端到端黑盒模型。

Abstract: Assistive robots operating in unstructured environments must understand not only what objects are, but what they can be used for. This requires grounding language-based action queries to objects that both afford the requested function and can be physically retrieved. Existing approaches often rely on black-box models or fixed affordance labels, limiting transparency, controllability, and reliability for human-facing applications. We introduce CRAFT-E, a modular neuro-symbolic framework that composes a structured verb-property-object knowledge graph with visual-language alignment and energy-based grasp reasoning. The system generates interpretable grounding paths that expose the factors influencing object selection and incorporates grasp feasibility as an integral part of affordance inference. We further construct a benchmark dataset with unified annotations for verb-object compatibility, segmentation, and grasp candidates, and deploy the full pipeline on a physical robot. CRAFT-E achieves competitive performance in static scenes, ImageNet-based functional retrieval, and real-world trials involving 20 verbs and 39 objects. The framework remains robust under perceptual noise and provides transparent, component-level diagnostics. By coupling symbolic reasoning with embodied perception, CRAFT-E offers an interpretable and customizable alternative to end-to-end models for affordance-grounded object selection, supporting trustworthy decision-making in assistive robotic systems.

中文标题: CRAFT-E：用于具身可供性接地的神经符号框架

中文摘要: 在非结构化环境中运行的辅助机器人不仅需要理解物体是什么，还需要理解它们可以用于什么目的。这需要将基于语言的动作查询接地到既能够提供所请求功能又能够被物理检索的物体上。现有方法通常依赖于黑盒模型或固定的可供性标签，限制了面向人类应用的透明度、可控性和可靠性。我们引入了CRAFT-E，这是一个模块化的神经符号框架，它将结构化的动词-属性-对象知识图与视觉语言对齐和基于能量的抓取推理相结合。该系统生成可解释的接地路径，揭示影响对象选择的因素，并将抓取可行性作为可供性推理的组成部分。我们进一步构建了一个具有统一注释的基准数据集，用于动词-对象兼容性、分割和抓取候选，并在物理机器人上部署了完整的流程。CRAFT-E在静态场景、基于ImageNet的功能检索以及涉及20个动词和39个物体的真实世界试验中实现了有竞争力的性能。该框架在感知噪声下保持鲁棒性，并提供透明的组件级诊断。通过将符号推理与具身感知相结合，CRAFT-E为可供性接地的对象选择提供了一个可解释和可定制的端到端模型替代方案，支持辅助机器人系统中的可信决策。

### [90] [Sliding Mode Control and Subspace Stabilization Methodology for the Orbital Stabilization of Periodic Trajectories](https://arxiv.org/abs/2512.04249)
*Maksim Surov,Leonid Freidovich*

Main category: cs.RO

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种结合滑模控制和子空间稳定化的方法，用于欠驱动机械系统中周期轨迹的轨道稳定化。该方法避免了计算密集的周期LQR问题，提高了对匹配扰动的鲁棒性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 欠驱动机械系统中周期轨迹的轨道稳定化是一个具有挑战性的问题。传统方法如周期LQR计算成本高，且对扰动敏感。需要一种更高效、鲁棒的方法来实现轨道稳定化。

Method: 1. 首先进行部分反馈线性化和稳定化；2. 计算沿参考轨道的横向线性化，得到具有稳定子空间的周期线性时变系统；3. 使用滑模控制将轨迹驱动到该稳定子空间。

Result: 该方法成功实现了周期轨迹的轨道稳定化，避免了计算密集的周期LQR问题，提高了对匹配扰动的鲁棒性。在蝴蝶机器人上的实验验证了该方法的有效性。

Conclusion: 提出的滑模控制与子空间稳定化相结合的方法为欠驱动机械系统中周期轨迹的轨道稳定化提供了一种高效、鲁棒的解决方案，在实验中得到验证。

Abstract: This paper presents a combined sliding-mode control and subspace stabilization methodology for orbital stabilization of periodic trajectories in underactuated mechanical systems with one degree of underactuation. The approach starts with partial feedback linearization and stabilization. Then, transverse linearization along the reference orbit is computed, resulting in a periodic linear time-varying system with a stable subspace. Sliding-mode control drives trajectories toward this subspace. The proposed design avoids solving computationally intensive periodic LQR problems and improves robustness to matched disturbances. The methodology is validated through experiments on the Butterfly robot.

中文标题: 周期轨迹轨道稳定化的滑模控制与子空间稳定化方法

中文摘要: 本文提出了一种结合滑模控制和子空间稳定化的方法，用于单自由度欠驱动机械系统中周期轨迹的轨道稳定化。该方法首先进行部分反馈线性化和稳定化，然后计算沿参考轨道的横向线性化，得到一个具有稳定子空间的周期线性时变系统。滑模控制将轨迹驱动到该子空间。所提出的设计避免了求解计算密集的周期LQR问题，并提高了对匹配扰动的鲁棒性。该方法在蝴蝶机器人上通过实验进行了验证。

### [91] [Driving Beyond Privilege: Distilling Dense-Reward Knowledge into Sparse-Reward Policies](https://arxiv.org/abs/2512.04279)
*Feeza Khan Khanzada,Jaerock Kwon*

Main category: cs.RO

TL;DR: 提出奖励特权世界模型蒸馏框架，通过教师模型利用密集特权奖励学习丰富动态模型，然后将其潜在动态蒸馏到仅使用稀疏任务奖励训练的学生模型中，在自动驾驶任务中实现更好的泛化性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在自动驾驶仿真中，密集奖励（如车道几何、违规、碰撞时间）可以加速强化学习，但直接在这些信号上训练的策略容易过拟合，在稀疏目标（如路线完成、无碰撞超车）上泛化能力差。需要利用密集奖励的优势而不继承其对部署指标的错位。

Method: 提出奖励特权世界模型蒸馏框架：1）教师DreamerV3智能体使用密集特权奖励训练；2）仅将教师的潜在动态蒸馏到学生模型中，学生仅使用稀疏任务奖励训练。师生共享相同观测空间（语义鸟瞰图），特权信息仅通过教师奖励进入，学生不模仿教师动作或价值估计，而是通过正则化使其世界模型匹配教师潜在动态，策略从稀疏成功/失败信号从头学习。

Result: 在CARLA车道跟随和超车基准测试中，稀疏奖励学生模型优于密集奖励教师模型和从头训练的稀疏奖励基线。在未见车道跟随路线上，成功率比密集教师提高约23%，同时保持相当或更好的安全性。在超车任务中，学生在训练路线上保持接近完美的性能，在未见路线上成功率提高高达27倍，车道保持能力也得到改善。

Conclusion: 密集奖励可用于学习更丰富的动态模型，同时使部署策略严格针对稀疏、与部署对齐的目标进行优化。奖励特权蒸馏框架成功利用了密集奖励的稳定性和加速优势，避免了其对部署指标的错位问题。

Abstract: We study how to exploit dense simulator-defined rewards in vision-based autonomous driving without inheriting their misalignment with deployment metrics. In realistic simulators such as CARLA, privileged state (e.g., lane geometry, infractions, time-to-collision) can be converted into dense rewards that stabilize and accelerate model-based reinforcement learning, but policies trained directly on these signals often overfit and fail to generalize when evaluated on sparse objectives such as route completion and collision-free overtaking. We propose reward-privileged world model distillation, a two-stage framework in which a teacher DreamerV3-style agent is first trained with a dense privileged reward, and only its latent dynamics are distilled into a student trained solely on sparse task rewards. Teacher and student share the same observation space (semantic bird's-eye-view images); privileged information enters only through the teacher's reward, and the student does not imitate the teacher's actions or value estimates. Instead, the student's world model is regularized to match the teacher's latent dynamics while its policy is learned from scratch on sparse success/failure signals. In CARLA lane-following and overtaking benchmarks, sparse-reward students outperform both dense-reward teachers and sparse-from-scratch baselines. On unseen lane-following routes, reward-privileged distillation improves success by about 23 percent relative to the dense teacher while maintaining comparable or better safety. On overtaking, students retain near-perfect performance on training routes and achieve up to a 27x improvement in success on unseen routes, with improved lane keeping. These results show that dense rewards can be leveraged to learn richer dynamics models while keeping the deployed policy optimized strictly for sparse, deployment-aligned objectives.

中文标题: 超越特权驾驶：将密集奖励知识蒸馏到稀疏奖励策略中

中文摘要: 我们研究如何在基于视觉的自动驾驶中利用密集仿真器定义的奖励，而不继承其对部署指标的错位。在CARLA等真实仿真器中，特权状态（如车道几何、违规、碰撞时间）可转换为密集奖励，稳定并加速基于模型的强化学习，但直接在这些信号上训练的策略在评估稀疏目标（如路线完成和无碰撞超车）时经常过拟合且泛化能力差。我们提出奖励特权世界模型蒸馏，一个两阶段框架：首先使用密集特权奖励训练教师DreamerV3智能体，然后仅将其潜在动态蒸馏到仅使用稀疏任务奖励训练的学生中。师生共享相同观测空间（语义鸟瞰图）；特权信息仅通过教师奖励进入，学生不模仿教师的动作或价值估计。相反，学生的世界模型通过正则化匹配教师的潜在动态，而其策略从稀疏成功/失败信号从头学习。在CARLA车道跟随和超车基准测试中，稀疏奖励学生优于密集奖励教师和从头训练的稀疏奖励基线。在未见车道跟随路线上，奖励特权蒸馏比密集教师提高约23%的成功率，同时保持相当或更好的安全性。在超车任务中，学生在训练路线上保持接近完美的性能，在未见路线上实现高达27倍的成功率提升，并改善车道保持。这些结果表明，密集奖励可用于学习更丰富的动态模型，同时使部署策略严格针对稀疏、与部署对齐的目标进行优化。

</details>


### [92] [Vertical Planetary Landing on Sloped Terrain Using Optical Flow Divergence Estimates](https://arxiv.org/abs/2512.04373)
*Hann Woei Ho,Ye Zhou*

Main category: cs.RO

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种基于光学流散度估计的垂直行星着陆控制策略，用于斜坡地形着陆。通过使用两个局部流散度估计来调节推力和姿态，采用增量非线性动态反演处理非线性特性，实现了小型航天器在斜坡上的稳定自主着陆。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 小型轻量级航天器（如旋翼机和着陆器）在斜坡地形上自主着陆面临重大挑战。这些飞行器处理能力和有效载荷有限，使得先进的深度学习方法和大重量传感器不实用。受蜜蜂等飞行昆虫的启发，它们仅依靠光学流就能实现卓越的着陆性能，通过调节流散度（垂直速度与高度的比值）实现平滑着陆。然而，将这种生物启发策略应用于斜坡地形着陆存在两个关键问题：全局流散度估计会掩盖地形倾斜度，以及基于散度的非线性控制在使用传统控制器时可能导致不稳定。

Method: 本文提出了一种非线性控制策略，利用两个不同的局部流散度估计来调节垂直着陆过程中的推力和姿态。控制律基于增量非线性动态反演（INDI）来应对非线性流散度。推力控制通过保持局部流散度估计的平均值为常数来确保平滑垂直下降，而姿态控制则通过利用两个估计值的差异来使飞行器在触地时与倾斜表面对齐。该方法使用简化的2D航天器模型在不同坡度和散度设定点下进行数值仿真评估。

Result: 数值仿真结果表明，调节平均散度能够实现速度和高度呈指数衰减的稳定着陆，而利用散度差异能够有效实现与倾斜地形的对齐。该方法在各种斜坡条件下都表现出良好的性能，为小型航天器提供了可靠的着陆策略。

Conclusion: 该方法提供了一种稳健、低资源消耗的着陆策略，增强了小型航天器自主行星任务的可行性。通过结合生物启发的光学流散度调节和增量非线性动态反演控制，成功解决了斜坡地形着陆中的关键挑战，为资源受限的航天器提供了实用的解决方案。

Abstract: Autonomous landing on sloped terrain poses significant challenges for small, lightweight spacecraft, such as rotorcraft and landers. These vehicles have limited processing capability and payload capacity, which makes advanced deep learning methods and heavy sensors impractical. Flying insects, such as bees, achieve remarkable landings with minimal neural and sensory resources, relying heavily on optical flow. By regulating flow divergence, a measure of vertical velocity divided by height, they perform smooth landings in which velocity and height decay exponentially together. However, adapting this bio-inspired strategy for spacecraft landings on sloped terrain presents two key challenges: global flow-divergence estimates obscure terrain inclination, and the nonlinear nature of divergence-based control can lead to instability when using conventional controllers. This paper proposes a nonlinear control strategy that leverages two distinct local flow divergence estimates to regulate both thrust and attitude during vertical landings. The control law is formulated based on Incremental Nonlinear Dynamic Inversion to handle the nonlinear flow divergence. The thrust control ensures a smooth vertical descent by keeping a constant average of the local flow divergence estimates, while the attitude control aligns the vehicle with the inclined surface at touchdown by exploiting their difference. The approach is evaluated in numerical simulations using a simplified 2D spacecraft model across varying slopes and divergence setpoints. Results show that regulating the average divergence yields stable landings with exponential decay of velocity and height, and using the divergence difference enables effective alignment with inclined terrain. Overall, the method offers a robust, low-resource landing strategy that enhances the feasibility of autonomous planetary missions with small spacecraft.

中文标题: 基于光学流散度估计的斜坡地形垂直行星着陆

中文摘要: 在斜坡地形上进行自主着陆对小型轻量级航天器（如旋翼机和着陆器）构成了重大挑战。这些飞行器处理能力和有效载荷有限，使得先进的深度学习方法和重型传感器不切实际。飞行昆虫（如蜜蜂）凭借最小的神经和感官资源实现了卓越的着陆性能，主要依赖光学流。通过调节流散度（垂直速度与高度的比值），它们实现了速度和高度呈指数衰减的平滑着陆。然而，将这种生物启发策略应用于斜坡地形着陆存在两个关键挑战：全局流散度估计会掩盖地形倾斜度，以及基于散度的非线性控制在使用传统控制器时可能导致不稳定。本文提出了一种非线性控制策略，利用两个不同的局部流散度估计来调节垂直着陆过程中的推力和姿态。控制律基于增量非线性动态反演来处理非线性流散度。推力控制通过保持局部流散度估计的平均值为常数来确保平滑垂直下降，而姿态控制则通过利用两个估计值的差异来使飞行器在触地时与倾斜表面对齐。该方法使用简化的2D航天器模型在不同坡度和散度设定点下进行数值仿真评估。结果表明，调节平均散度能够实现速度和高度呈指数衰减的稳定着陆，而利用散度差异能够有效实现与倾斜地形的对齐。总体而言，该方法提供了一种稳健、低资源消耗的着陆策略，增强了小型航天器自主行星任务的可行性。

### [93] [FALCON: Actively Decoupled Visuomotor Policies for Loco-Manipulation with Foundation-Model-Based Coordination](https://arxiv.org/abs/2512.04381)
*Chengyang He,Ge Sun,Yue Bai,Junkai Lu,Jiadong Zhao,Guillaume Sartoretti*

Main category: cs.RO

TL;DR: FALCON是一个用于移动操作任务的框架，通过视觉语言基础模型协调解耦的移动和操作策略，解决了单一策略处理异构观察时性能下降的问题。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 移动操作任务中，单一策略需要融合移动和操作两种异构观察，这会导致性能下降。现有方法难以有效协调解耦的子系统。

Method: 将移动和操作解耦为两个专门的视觉运动策略，通过视觉语言基础模型编码全局观察和语言指令作为共享潜在嵌入来协调两个策略。引入阶段进度头进行任务阶段推断，并采用协调感知对比损失编码跨子系统兼容性。

Result: 在两个需要导航、精确末端执行器放置和紧密基座-手臂协调的移动操作任务中，FALCON超越了集中式和去中心化基线，在分布外场景中表现出更好的鲁棒性和泛化能力。

Conclusion: FALCON通过基础模型协调的解耦策略框架，有效解决了移动操作中的异构观察融合问题，实现了更好的任务性能和泛化能力。

Abstract: We present FoundAtion-model-guided decoupled LoCO-maNipulation visuomotor policies (FALCON), a framework for loco-manipulation that combines modular diffusion policies with a vision-language foundation model as the coordinator. Our approach explicitly decouples locomotion and manipulation into two specialized visuomotor policies, allowing each subsystem to rely on its own observations. This mitigates the performance degradation that arise when a single policy is forced to fuse heterogeneous, potentially mismatched observations from locomotion and manipulation. Our key innovation lies in restoring coordination between these two independent policies through a vision-language foundation model, which encodes global observations and language instructions into a shared latent embedding conditioning both diffusion policies. On top of this backbone, we introduce a phase-progress head that uses textual descriptions of task stages to infer discrete phase and continuous progress estimates without manual phase labels. To further structure the latent space, we incorporate a coordination-aware contrastive loss that explicitly encodes cross-subsystem compatibility between arm and base actions. We evaluate FALCON on two challenging loco-manipulation tasks requiring navigation, precise end-effector placement, and tight base-arm coordination. Results show that it surpasses centralized and decentralized baselines while exhibiting improved robustness and generalization to out-of-distribution scenarios.

中文标题: FALCON：基于基础模型协调的解耦视觉运动策略用于移动操作

中文摘要: 我们提出了基于基础模型引导的解耦移动操作视觉运动策略（FALCON），这是一个将模块化扩散策略与作为协调器的视觉语言基础模型相结合的移动操作框架。我们的方法明确地将移动和操作解耦为两个专门的视觉运动策略，允许每个子系统依赖自己的观察。这减轻了当单一策略被迫融合来自移动和操作的异构、可能不匹配的观察时出现的性能下降。我们的关键创新在于通过视觉语言基础模型恢复这两个独立策略之间的协调，该模型将全局观察和语言指令编码为共享的潜在嵌入，用于调节两个扩散策略。在此基础之上，我们引入了一个阶段进度头，使用任务阶段的文本描述来推断离散阶段和连续进度估计，而无需手动阶段标签。为了进一步结构化潜在空间，我们采用了协调感知对比损失，明确编码手臂和基座动作之间的跨子系统兼容性。我们在两个需要导航、精确末端执行器放置和紧密基座-手臂协调的挑战性移动操作任务上评估FALCON。结果表明，它超越了集中式和去中心化基线，同时在分布外场景中表现出改进的鲁棒性和泛化能力。

</details>


### [94] [Development of a 15-Degree-of-Freedom Bionic Hand with Cable-Driven Transmission and Distributed Actuation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2512.04399)

Main category: cs.RO

TL;DR: 开发了一种15自由度的仿生手，采用缆绳驱动传输和分布式驱动设计，仅用15个电机实现15个自由度，显著减少了传统缆绳驱动系统所需的电机数量，同时保持了与人手一致的尺寸和运动性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在机器人手研究中，如何在保持与人手一致的尺寸和自由度的同时最小化执行器数量是一个基本挑战。传统缆绳驱动系统通常需要大量电机，导致结构复杂、重量增加。

Method: 受人手运动学配置和肌肉分布策略的启发，提出了一种新型15自由度灵巧机器人手。采用新的腱驱动机制，在手臂中集成5个电机提供强大抓握力，手掌中安装10个小电机支持精细操作任务。开发了相应的关节传感和电机驱动电气系统。

Result: 整个系统仅重1.4公斤，结合了轻量化和高性能特点。实验表明，该仿生手展现出卓越的灵巧性和强大的抓握能力，在机器人操作任务中显示出显著潜力。

Conclusion: 该研究成功开发了一种创新的15自由度仿生手，通过分布式驱动设计和优化的缆绳传输机制，在减少电机数量的同时保持了高性能，为机器人操作任务提供了有前景的解决方案。

Abstract: In robotic hand research, minimizing the number of actuators while maintaining human-hand-consistent dimensions and degrees of freedom constitutes a fundamental challenge. Drawing bio-inspiration from human hand kinematic configurations and muscle distribution strategies, this work proposes a novel 15-DoF dexterous robotic hand, with detailed analysis of its mechanical architecture, electrical system, and control system. The bionic hand employs a new tendon-driven mechanism, significantly reducing the number of motors required by traditional tendon-driven systems while enhancing motion performance and simplifying the mechanical structure. This design integrates five motors in the forearm to provide strong gripping force, while ten small motors are installed in the palm to support fine manipulation tasks. Additionally, a corresponding joint sensing and motor driving electrical system was developed to ensure efficient control and feedback. The entire system weighs only 1.4kg, combining lightweight and high-performance features. Through experiments, the bionic hand exhibited exceptional dexterity and robust grasping capabilities, demonstrating significant potential for robotic manipulation tasks.

### [95] [RoboBPP: Benchmarking Robotic Online Bin Packing with Physics-based Simulation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2512.04415)
*Zhoufeng Wang,Hang Zhao,Juzhan Xu,Shishun Zhang,Zeyu Xiong,Ruizhen Hu,Chenyang Zhu,Kai Xu*

Main category: cs.RO

TL;DR: RoboBPP是一个用于机器人在线装箱的基准测试系统，集成了物理仿真器、真实工业数据集和全面的评估指标，解决了该领域缺乏标准化测试环境的问题。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前机器人装箱领域存在三个主要问题：1）缺乏统一的基准测试系统，导致问题设置、数据集和评估指标不一致；2）直接在真实硬件上测试成本高昂；3）现有研究多使用与真实工业数据分布不同的合成数据集。

Method: 1）开发基于物理的仿真环境，包含真实尺度的机械臂和箱子；2）从三个真实工业场景（装配线、物流包装、家具制造）收集数据集；3）设计三个测试设置和扩展的评估指标（包括结构稳定性和操作安全性）；4）建立评分系统和可视化工具。

Result: 创建了一个完全开源的基准测试系统，包含物理仿真器、真实工业数据集、综合评估指标、可视化工具和在线排行榜，为机器人装箱研究提供了可重复和可扩展的测试平台。

Conclusion: RoboBPP填补了机器人在线装箱领域基准测试的空白，通过物理仿真和真实工业数据确保了算法的实际部署可行性，为未来的研究和工业应用提供了标准化评估框架。

Abstract: Physical feasibility in 3D bin packing is a key requirement in modern industrial logistics and robotic automation. With the growing adoption of industrial automation, online bin packing has gained increasing attention. However, inconsistencies in problem settings, test datasets, and evaluation metrics have hindered progress in the field, and there is a lack of a comprehensive benchmarking system. Direct testing on real hardware is costly, and building a realistic simulation environment is also challenging. To address these limitations, we introduce RoboBPP, a benchmarking system designed for robotic online bin packing. RoboBPP integrates a physics-based simulator to assess physical feasibility. In our simulation environment, we introduce a robotic arm and boxes at real-world scales to replicate real industrial packing workflows. By simulating conditions that arise in real industrial applications, we ensure that evaluated algorithms are practically deployable. In addition, prior studies often rely on synthetic datasets whose distributions differ from real-world industrial data. To address this issue, we collect three datasets from real industrial workflows, including assembly-line production, logistics packing, and furniture manufacturing. The benchmark comprises three carefully designed test settings and extends existing evaluation metrics with new metrics for structural stability and operational safety. We design a scoring system and derive a range of insights from the evaluation results. RoboBPP is fully open-source and is equipped with visualization tools and an online leaderboard, providing a reproducible and extensible foundation for future research and industrial applications (https://robot-bin-packing-benchmark.github.io).

中文标题: RoboBPP：基于物理仿真的机器人在线装箱基准测试系统

中文摘要: 3D装箱中的物理可行性是现代工业物流和机器人自动化的关键要求。随着工业自动化的日益普及，在线装箱问题受到越来越多的关注。然而，问题设置、测试数据集和评估指标的不一致性阻碍了该领域的发展，并且缺乏全面的基准测试系统。直接在真实硬件上进行测试成本高昂，构建真实的仿真环境也具有挑战性。为了解决这些局限性，我们引入了RoboBPP，一个专为机器人在线装箱设计的基准测试系统。RoboBPP集成了基于物理的仿真器来评估物理可行性。在我们的仿真环境中，我们引入了真实世界尺度的机械臂和箱子，以复制真实的工业装箱工作流程。通过模拟真实工业应用中出现的条件，我们确保评估的算法具有实际部署可行性。此外，先前的研究通常依赖于分布与真实工业数据不同的合成数据集。为了解决这个问题，我们从真实的工业工作流程中收集了三个数据集，包括装配线生产、物流包装和家具制造。该基准测试包含三个精心设计的测试设置，并通过新的结构稳定性和操作安全性指标扩展了现有的评估指标。我们设计了一个评分系统，并从评估结果中得出一系列见解。RoboBPP完全开源，配备了可视化工具和在线排行榜，为未来的研究和工业应用提供了可重复和可扩展的基础（https://robot-bin-packing-benchmark.github.io）。

### [96] [Vision-Language-Action Models for Selective Robotic Disassembly: A Case Study on Critical Component Extraction from Desktops](https://arxiv.org/abs/2512.04446)
*Chang Liu,Sibo Tian,Sara Behdad,Xiao Liang,Minghui Zheng*

Main category: cs.RO

TL;DR: 本文研究了视觉-语言-动作模型在选择性机器人拆解中的应用，通过收集RAM和CPU拆解数据集微调OpenVLA模型，发现纯VLA模型能完成早期步骤但难以处理关键精细操作，而结合规则控制器的混合策略能成功完成整个拆解任务。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 自动化拆解废旧台式机中的关键组件（如RAM、CPU、硬盘）面临挑战，因为这些产品具有高度变异性，拆解需要精确、灵巧的序列操作。现有机器人拆解流程需要分阶段显式建模，限制了泛化能力。视觉-语言-动作模型为端到端机器人操作提供了新思路，但其在复杂拆解任务中的可行性尚未充分探索。

Method: 收集了机器人RAM和CPU拆解的自定义数据集，用于微调两种成熟的VLA方法（OpenVLA和OpenVLA-OFT）。将整个拆解任务分解为多个小步骤，并测试纯VLA模型与结合规则控制器的混合策略的性能。

Result: 微调后的VLA模型能够忠实完成多个早期拆解步骤，但在某些关键精细子任务上表现不佳，导致任务失败。然而，简单的混合策略（VLA结合规则控制器）能够成功执行整个拆解操作。

Conclusion: VLA模型在处理机器人废旧产品拆解所需的灵巧性和精确性方面仍存在局限性。混合策略展示了当前技术水平的可行性，为未来研究提供了方向，以解决当前挑战并推进端到端机器人自动化拆解的发展。

Abstract: Automating disassembly of critical components from end-of-life (EoL) desktops, such as high-value items like RAM modules and CPUs, as well as sensitive parts like hard disk drives, remains challenging due to the inherent variability and uncertainty of these products. Moreover, their disassembly requires sequential, precise, and dexterous operations, further increasing the complexity of automation. Current robotic disassembly processes are typically divided into several stages: perception, sequence planning, task planning, motion planning, and manipulation. Each stage requires explicit modeling, which limits generalization to unfamiliar scenarios. Recent development of vision-language-action (VLA) models has presented an end-to-end approach for general robotic manipulation tasks. Although VLAs have demonstrated promising performance on simple tasks, the feasibility of applying such models to complex disassembly remains largely unexplored. In this paper, we collected a customized dataset for robotic RAM and CPU disassembly and used it to fine-tune two well-established VLA approaches, OpenVLA and OpenVLA-OFT, as a case study. We divided the whole disassembly task into several small steps, and our preliminary experimental results indicate that the fine-tuned VLA models can faithfully complete multiple early steps but struggle with certain critical subtasks, leading to task failure. However, we observed that a simple hybrid strategy that combines VLA with a rule-based controller can successfully perform the entire disassembly operation. These findings highlight the current limitations of VLA models in handling the dexterity and precision required for robotic EoL product disassembly. By offering a detailed analysis of the observed results, this study provides insights that may inform future research to address current challenges and advance end-to-end robotic automated disassembly.

中文标题: 视觉-语言-动作模型在选择性机器人拆解中的应用：以台式机关键组件提取为例的研究

中文摘要: 自动化拆解废旧台式机中的关键组件，如高价值的内存模块和CPU，以及敏感的硬盘驱动器等，仍然具有挑战性，因为这些产品具有固有的变异性和不确定性。此外，它们的拆解需要顺序、精确和灵巧的操作，进一步增加了自动化的复杂性。当前的机器人拆解流程通常分为几个阶段：感知、序列规划、任务规划、运动规划和操作。每个阶段都需要显式建模，这限制了其对陌生场景的泛化能力。最近视觉-语言-动作模型的发展为通用机器人操作任务提供了一种端到端方法。尽管VLA模型在简单任务上表现出了良好的性能，但将此类模型应用于复杂拆解的可行性在很大程度上尚未得到探索。在本文中，我们收集了一个用于机器人RAM和CPU拆解的自定义数据集，并以此作为案例研究，微调了两种成熟的VLA方法：OpenVLA和OpenVLA-OFT。我们将整个拆解任务分解为几个小步骤，初步实验结果表明，微调后的VLA模型能够忠实完成多个早期步骤，但在某些关键子任务上存在困难，导致任务失败。然而，我们观察到，将VLA与基于规则的控制器相结合的简单混合策略能够成功执行整个拆解操作。这些发现突显了VLA模型在处理机器人废旧产品拆解所需的灵巧性和精确性方面的当前局限性。通过对观察结果进行详细分析，本研究提供了可能为未来研究提供信息的见解，以解决当前挑战并推进端到端机器人自动化拆解。

</details>


### [97] [Open-Ended Goal Inference through Actions and Language for Human-Robot Collaboration](https://arxiv.org/abs/2512.04453)
*Debasmita Ghose,Oz Gitelson,Marynel Vazquez,Brian Scassellati*

Main category: cs.RO

TL;DR: BALI方法通过整合语言偏好和观察行动来推断开放式目标，仅在信息增益超过中断成本时提问，并在协作烹饪任务中表现出更好的稳定性和更少错误。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 人机协作中，人类目标往往模糊、难以表达或不属于固定集合。现有方法要么限制在预定义目标集，要么只依赖行动或指令，导致在现实交互中表现脆弱。

Method: 提出BALI方法，将自然语言偏好与观察到的行动整合到后退时域规划树中，结合语言和行动线索，智能地提出澄清问题（当信息增益超过中断成本时），并选择支持性行动。

Result: 在协作烹饪任务中评估，BALI相比基线方法产生了更稳定的目标预测和显著更少的错误，能够处理对机器人新颖且无界的目标。

Conclusion: BALI通过整合语言和行动信息进行开放式目标推理，提高了人机协作的鲁棒性和效率，在现实世界交互中表现优于仅依赖单一模态的方法。

Abstract: To collaborate with humans, robots must infer goals that are often ambiguous, difficult to articulate, or not drawn from a fixed set. Prior approaches restrict inference to a predefined goal set, rely only on observed actions, or depend exclusively on explicit instructions, making them brittle in real-world interactions. We present BALI (Bidirectional Action-Language Inference) for goal prediction, a method that integrates natural language preferences with observed human actions in a receding-horizon planning tree. BALI combines language and action cues from the human, asks clarifying questions only when the expected information gain from the answer outweighs the cost of interruption, and selects supportive actions that align with inferred goals. We evaluate the approach in collaborative cooking tasks, where goals may be novel to the robot and unbounded. Compared to baselines, BALI yields more stable goal predictions and significantly fewer mistakes.

中文标题: 通过行动和语言进行开放式目标推理以实现人机协作

中文摘要: 为了与人类协作，机器人必须推断那些通常模糊、难以表达或不属于固定集合的目标。先前的方法将推理限制在预定义的目标集合内，仅依赖观察到的行动，或完全依赖明确的指令，这使得它们在现实世界交互中显得脆弱。我们提出了BALI（双向行动-语言推理）用于目标预测，该方法将自然语言偏好与观察到的人类行动整合到一个后退时域规划树中。BALI结合了来自人类的语言和行动线索，仅当从答案中获得的预期信息增益超过中断成本时才提出澄清问题，并选择与推断目标一致的支持性行动。我们在协作烹饪任务中评估了该方法，其中目标对机器人可能是新颖且无界的。与基线相比，BALI产生了更稳定的目标预测和显著更少的错误。

### [98] [One Ring to Rule Them All: Constrained Distributional Control for Massive-Scale Heterogeneous Robotic Ensemble Systems](https://arxiv.org/abs/2512.04502)
*Andres Arias,Wei Zhang,Haoyu Qian,Jr-Shin Li,Chuangchuang Sun*

Main category: cs.RO

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种约束集群控制框架，通过矩核变换将异构机器人系统的动态和约束映射到矩空间，使用单个共享控制器实现大规模机器人集群的安全控制。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统集群控制方法难以处理大规模异构机器人系统在复杂环境约束下的控制问题，需要一种能够统一处理参数化、异构系统并满足状态和环境约束的框架。

Method: 开发矩核变换将参数化集群动态映射到核空间的矩系统；将状态空间约束（航点、障碍物）转换到矩空间；使用信号时序逻辑编码复杂任务；通过约束优化合成单个共享控制器。

Result: 提出的框架能够有效控制大规模异构机器人集群，在仿真和硬件实验中实现了安全高效的约束环境导航，验证了方法的可行性和有效性。

Conclusion: 该约束集群控制框架为大规模异构机器人系统的安全控制提供了统一解决方案，通过矩空间变换和共享控制器实现了复杂环境下的高效群体控制。

Abstract: Ensemble control aims to steer a population of dynamical systems using a shared control input. This paper introduces a constrained ensemble control framework for parameterized, heterogeneous robotic systems operating under state and environmental constraints, such as obstacle avoidance. We develop a moment kernel transform that maps the parameterized ensemble dynamics to the moment system in a kernel space, enabling the characterization of population-level behavior. The state-space constraints, such as polyhedral waypoints to be visited and obstacles to be avoided, are also transformed into the moment space, leading to a unified formulation for safe, large-scale ensemble control. Expressive signal temporal logic specifications are employed to encode complex visit-avoid tasks, which are achieved through a single shared controller synthesized from our constrained ensemble control formulation. Simulation and hardware experiments demonstrate the effectiveness of the proposed approach in safely and efficiently controlling robotic ensembles within constrained environments.

中文标题: 一统全局：面向大规模异构机器人集群系统的约束分布控制

中文摘要: 集群控制旨在使用共享控制输入来引导一组动态系统。本文提出了一种约束集群控制框架，用于参数化、异构的机器人系统在状态和环境约束（如避障）下的操作。我们开发了一种矩核变换，将参数化的集群动态映射到核空间中的矩系统，从而能够表征群体级行为。状态空间约束，如需要访问的多面体航点和需要避开的障碍物，也被转换到矩空间，形成了安全、大规模集群控制的统一公式。我们采用表达性信号时序逻辑规范来编码复杂的访问-避让任务，这些任务通过从我们的约束集群控制公式合成的单个共享控制器实现。仿真和硬件实验证明了所提出方法在约束环境中安全高效控制机器人集群的有效性。

### [99] [Bridging Simulation and Reality: Cross-Domain Transfer with Semantic 2D Gaussian Splatting](https://arxiv.org/abs/2512.04731)
*Jian Tang,Pu Pang,Haowen Sun,Chengzhong Ma,Xingyu Chen,Hua Huang,Xuguang Lan*

Main category: cs.RO

TL;DR: 提出语义2D高斯泼溅方法，通过提取物体中心、领域不变的空间特征来弥合仿真与现实之间的领域差距，显著提升机器人操作策略的仿真到现实迁移能力。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 机器人操作中的跨领域迁移面临仿真与现实环境之间存在显著领域差距的长期挑战。现有方法如领域随机化、适应和仿真-现实校准通常需要大量调优或无法泛化到未见场景。研究发现，如果在仿真策略训练中使用领域不变特征，并且在现实部署时能够提取并提供相同特征作为策略输入，就能有效弥合领域差距。

Method: 提出语义2D高斯泼溅方法，该方法构建多视角2D语义场，通过特征级高斯泼溅将其投影到统一的3D空间中。采用语义过滤机制去除不相关的背景内容，确保策略学习获得干净一致的输入。使用Diffusion Policy作为下游学习算法，在ManiSkill仿真环境中进行实验，然后在现实世界部署。

Result: 实验结果表明，S2GS显著提高了仿真到现实的迁移能力，在现实场景中保持高且稳定的任务性能。该方法有效弥合了领域差距，提升了策略的泛化能力。

Conclusion: 语义2D高斯泼溅方法通过提取领域不变的空间特征，成功解决了机器人操作中仿真到现实迁移的挑战，为跨领域策略泛化提供了有效解决方案。

Abstract: Cross-domain transfer in robotic manipulation remains a longstanding challenge due to the significant domain gap between simulated and real-world environments. Existing methods such as domain randomization, adaptation, and sim-real calibration often require extensive tuning or fail to generalize to unseen scenarios. To address this issue, we observe that if domain-invariant features are utilized during policy training in simulation, and the same features can be extracted and provided as the input to policy during real-world deployment, the domain gap can be effectively bridged, leading to significantly improved policy generalization. Accordingly, we propose Semantic 2D Gaussian Splatting (S2GS), a novel representation method that extracts object-centric, domain-invariant spatial features. S2GS constructs multi-view 2D semantic fields and projects them into a unified 3D space via feature-level Gaussian splatting. A semantic filtering mechanism removes irrelevant background content, ensuring clean and consistent inputs for policy learning. To evaluate the effectiveness of S2GS, we adopt Diffusion Policy as the downstream learning algorithm and conduct experiments in the ManiSkill simulation environment, followed by real-world deployment. Results demonstrate that S2GS significantly improves sim-to-real transferability, maintaining high and stable task performance in real-world scenarios.

中文标题: 弥合仿真与现实：基于语义2D高斯泼溅的跨领域迁移

中文摘要: 由于仿真与现实环境之间存在显著领域差距，机器人操作中的跨领域迁移仍然是一个长期挑战。现有方法如领域随机化、适应和仿真-现实校准通常需要大量调优或无法泛化到未见场景。为解决这一问题，我们观察到，如果在仿真策略训练中使用领域不变特征，并且在现实部署时能够提取并提供相同特征作为策略输入，就能有效弥合领域差距，显著提升策略泛化能力。据此，我们提出语义2D高斯泼溅，这是一种新颖的表征方法，能够提取物体中心、领域不变的空间特征。S2GS构建多视角2D语义场，并通过特征级高斯泼溅将其投影到统一的3D空间中。语义过滤机制去除不相关的背景内容，确保策略学习获得干净一致的输入。为评估S2GS的有效性，我们采用Diffusion Policy作为下游学习算法，在ManiSkill仿真环境中进行实验，然后在现实世界部署。结果表明，S2GS显著提高了仿真到现实的迁移能力，在现实场景中保持高且稳定的任务性能。

### [100] [TEMPO-VINE: A Multi-Temporal Sensor Fusion Dataset for Localization and Mapping in Vineyards](https://arxiv.org/abs/2512.04772)

Abstract: In recent years, precision agriculture has been introducing groundbreaking innovations in the field, with a strong focus on automation. 中文摘要: 近年来，精准农业在田间引入了突破性创新，重点关注自动化。然而，机器人和自主导航的研究通常依赖于受控模拟或孤立的田间试验。缺乏真实的共同基准代表了在真实复杂农业条件下推广鲁棒自主系统的重大限制。葡萄园由于其动态特性提出了重大挑战，并且越来越吸引对自动化感兴趣的学术和工业利益相关者的关注。在此背景下，我们介绍了TEMPO-VINE数据集，这是一个专门为评估操作葡萄园环境中的传感器融合、同时定位与建图（SLAM）以及地点识别技术而设计的大规模多时相数据集。TEMPO-VINE是首个多模态公共数据集，汇集了不同价格水平的异构LiDAR、AHRS、RTK-GPS和相机在真实葡萄架和凉棚葡萄园中的数据，其中多行长度超过100米。在这项工作中，我们通过提供不同季节、植被生长阶段、地形和天气条件下的全面数据收集和地面真实轨迹，解决了农业数据集领域的关键空白。具有多次运行和重访的序列路径将促进农业领域传感器融合、定位、建图和地点识别解决方案的发展。数据集、处理工具和基准测试结果将在接受后在专用网页上提供。

### [101] [Using Machine Learning to Take Stay-or-Go Decisions in Data-driven Drone Missions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2512.04773)
*Giorgos Polychronis,Foivos Pournaropoulos,Christos D. Antonopoulos,Spyros Lalis*

Main category: cs.RO

TL;DR: 本文提出基于机器学习的无人机数据驱动任务决策方法，用于决定无人机在采集数据后是停留处理还是前往下一个兴趣点。通过分支预测和强化学习方法，显著优化了任务执行时间。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 无人机在数据驱动任务中面临"停留处理"与"前往下一点"的决策困境：如果停留处理但未发现需要后续行动的事件，则浪费时间；如果直接前往下一点但后续发现需要返回处理，则需额外飞行时间返回。现有回归方法性能有限，需要更智能的决策方法。

Method: 提出了两种机器学习方法：1）基于分支预测的方法，预测是否需要后续行动；2）基于强化学习的方法，学习最优决策策略。这些方法考虑了事件发生概率随时间变化的情况，并在多种场景下进行评估。

Result: 实验结果显示，提出的机器学习方法显著优于文献中的回归方法，最坏情况任务时间最多可提升4.1倍。同时，中位任务时间仅比具有完美事件概率知识的方法高出最多2.7%，表现接近最优。

Conclusion: 机器学习方法能够有效解决无人机数据驱动任务中的停留-离开决策问题，显著提升任务效率，特别是在事件概率随时间变化的复杂场景中表现出色。

Abstract: Drones are becoming indispensable in many application domains. In data-driven missions, besides sensing, the drone must process the collected data at runtime to decide whether additional action must be taken on the spot, before moving to the next point of interest. If processing does not reveal an event or situation that requires such an action, the drone has waited in vain instead of moving to the next point. If, however, the drone starts moving to the next point and it turns out that a follow-up action is needed at the previous point, it must spend time to fly-back. To take this decision, we propose different machine-learning methods based on branch prediction and reinforcement learning. We evaluate these methods for a wide range of scenarios where the probability of event occurrence changes with time. Our results show that the proposed methods consistently outperform the regression-based method proposed in the literature and can significantly improve the worst-case mission time by up to 4.1x. Also, the achieved median mission time is very close, merely up to 2.7% higher, to that of a method with perfect knowledge of the current underlying event probability at each point of interest.

中文标题: 使用机器学习进行数据驱动无人机任务中的停留或离开决策

中文摘要: 无人机在许多应用领域变得不可或缺。在数据驱动任务中，除了感知外，无人机必须在运行时处理收集的数据，以决定是否需要在现场采取额外行动，然后再前往下一个兴趣点。如果处理未发现需要此类行动的事件或情况，无人机就会白白等待而不是前往下一点。然而，如果无人机开始前往下一个点，结果发现前一个点需要后续行动，它就必须花费时间飞回。为了做出这一决策，我们提出了基于分支预测和强化学习的不同机器学习方法。我们在事件发生概率随时间变化的各种场景下评估这些方法。我们的结果表明，所提出的方法始终优于文献中提出的基于回归的方法，并且可以将最坏情况任务时间显著提高多达4.1倍。此外，所实现的中位任务时间非常接近，仅比在每个兴趣点具有当前基础事件概率完美知识的方法高出最多2.7%。

</details>


### [102] [Hoi! - A Multimodal Dataset for Force-Grounded, Cross-View Articulated Manipulation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2512.04884)
*Tim Engelbracht,René Zurbrügg,Matteo Wohlrapp,Martin Büchner,Abhinav Valada,Marc Pollefeys,Hermann Blum,Zuria Bauer*

Main category: cs.RO

TL;DR: 该论文提出了Hoi!数据集，这是一个用于力感知、跨视角关节操作的多模态数据集，包含3048个序列、381个关节对象和38个环境，涵盖人类手部、手持工具和机器人抓取器四种操作方式，提供同步的末端执行器力和触觉感知数据。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前交互理解研究主要依赖视觉信息，缺乏将视觉、动作和力感知相结合的多模态数据集。为了研究人类与机器人之间的视角转换，以及探索力感知等未被充分研究的模态，需要构建一个能够耦合"所见"、"所做"和"所感"的综合数据集。

Method: 构建了一个包含3048个操作序列的数据集，涵盖381个关节对象和38个环境。采用四种操作方式：1) 人类手部直接操作；2) 人类手部配戴腕部相机；3) 手持UMI夹持器；4) 定制Hoi!夹持器。工具实施例提供同步的末端执行器力和触觉感知，实现跨视角的多模态数据采集。

Result: 成功创建了一个全面的多模态数据集，提供了从视频到交互理解的完整视角。数据集支持评估方法在人类和机器人视角之间的迁移能力，并为力感知和预测等未充分探索的模态提供了研究基础。

Conclusion: Hoi!数据集为力感知、跨视角关节操作研究提供了重要资源，能够促进交互理解方法的发展，特别是人类与机器人视角转换以及多模态感知（包括力感知）的研究。

Abstract: We present a dataset for force-grounded, cross-view articulated manipulation that couples what is seen with what is done and what is felt during real human interaction. The dataset contains 3048 sequences across 381 articulated objects in 38 environments. Each object is operated under four embodiments - (i) human hand, (ii) human hand with a wrist-mounted camera, (iii) handheld UMI gripper, and (iv) a custom Hoi! gripper - where the tool embodiment provides synchronized end-effector forces and tactile sensing. Our dataset offers a holistic view of interaction understanding from video, enabling researchers to evaluate how well methods transfer between human and robotic viewpoints, but also investigate underexplored modalities such as force sensing and prediction.

中文标题: Hoi! - 一个用于力感知、跨视角关节操作的多模态数据集

中文摘要: 我们提出了一个用于力感知、跨视角关节操作的数据集，该数据集将真实人类交互过程中的所见、所做和所感耦合在一起。数据集包含38个环境中的381个关节对象的3048个操作序列。每个对象在四种操作方式下进行操作：(i) 人类手部，(ii) 配戴腕部相机的人类手部，(iii) 手持UMI夹持器，以及(iv) 定制的Hoi!夹持器 - 其中工具实施例提供同步的末端执行器力和触觉感知。我们的数据集提供了从视频到交互理解的完整视角，使研究人员能够评估方法在人类和机器人视角之间的迁移效果，同时探索力感知和预测等未被充分研究的模态。

### [103] [On Disturbance-Aware Minimum-Time Trajectory Planning: Evidence from Tests on a Dynamic Driving Simulator](https://arxiv.org/abs/2512.04917)
*Matteo Masoni,Vincenzo Palermo,Marco Gabiccini,Martino Gulisano,Giorgio Previati,Massimiliano Gobbi,Francesco Comolli,Gianpiero Mastinu,Massimo Guiggiani*

Main category: cs.RO

TL;DR: 该研究在动态驾驶模拟器中测试了三种扰动感知轨迹规划方法，发现摩擦极限鲁棒轨迹（FLC）能在仅略微增加圈时的情况下显著降低转向努力，为专业驾驶员提供了有效的训练工具和性能优化方案。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究旨在探索扰动感知、鲁棒性嵌入的参考轨迹在实际驾驶中的性能表现，特别是评估不同鲁棒性策略在圈时与转向努力之间的权衡，为专业驾驶员训练和轨迹规划提供实证依据。

Method: 使用作者最近提出的扰动感知最小圈时框架，生成三种参考轨迹：名义时间最优轨迹（NOM）、赛道极限鲁棒轨迹（TLC）和摩擦极限鲁棒轨迹（FLC）。通过两名专业驾驶员在动态模拟器中使用高性能车辆在虚拟赛道上执行这些轨迹，并与自由驾驶基线（NOREF）进行比较。评估指标包括圈时、转向努力、RMS横向偏差、速度误差和漂移角。

Result: 结果显示明显的LT-SE权衡关系：NOM获得最短圈时（平均约1:14.5）但转向努力最高；TLC转向努力最低但圈时最长（约1:15.5）；FLC位于效率前沿附近，转向努力显著低于NOM而圈时仅略微增加（约1:15.0）。NOREF的圈时和转向努力均最高，证实参考轨迹能改善驾驶性能。

Conclusion: 扰动感知轨迹规划（特别是FLC方法）能有效平衡圈时与转向努力，为专业驾驶员提供快速且稳定的参考轨迹。基于参考的规划显著优于自由驾驶，证明了其在驾驶训练和性能优化中的实用价值。

Abstract: This work investigates how disturbance-aware, robustness-embedded reference trajectories translate into driving performance when executed by professional drivers in a dynamic simulator. Three planned reference trajectories are compared against a free-driving baseline (NOREF) to assess trade-offs between lap time (LT) and steering effort (SE): NOM, the nominal time-optimal trajectory; TLC, a track-limit-robust trajectory obtained by tightening margins to the track edges; and FLC, a friction-limit-robust trajectory obtained by tightening against axle and tire saturation. All trajectories share the same minimum lap-time objective with a small steering-smoothness regularizer and are evaluated by two professional drivers using a high-performance car on a virtual track. The trajectories derive from a disturbance-aware minimum-lap-time framework recently proposed by the authors, where worst-case disturbance growth is propagated over a finite horizon and used to tighten tire-friction and track-limit constraints, preserving performance while providing probabilistic safety margins. LT and SE are used as performance indicators, while RMS lateral deviation, speed error, and drift angle characterize driving style. Results show a Pareto-like LT-SE trade-off: NOM yields the shortest LT but highest SE; TLC minimizes SE at the cost of longer LT; FLC lies near the efficient frontier, substantially reducing SE relative to NOM with only a small LT increase. Removing trajectory guidance (NOREF) increases both LT and SE, confirming that reference trajectories improve pace and control efficiency. Overall, the findings highlight reference-based and disturbance-aware planning, especially FLC, as effective tools for training and for achieving fast yet stable trajectories.

中文标题: 关于扰动感知最小时间轨迹规划的研究：基于动态驾驶模拟器的测试证据

中文摘要: 本研究探讨了扰动感知、鲁棒性嵌入的参考轨迹在专业驾驶员于动态模拟器中执行时的驾驶性能表现。通过比较三种规划的参考轨迹与自由驾驶基线（NOREF），评估了圈时（LT）与转向努力（SE）之间的权衡：NOM为名义时间最优轨迹；TLC是通过收紧赛道边缘裕度获得的赛道极限鲁棒轨迹；FLC是通过收紧车轴和轮胎饱和裕度获得的摩擦极限鲁棒轨迹。所有轨迹共享相同的最小圈时目标并带有小的转向平滑正则化项，由两名专业驾驶员在虚拟赛道上使用高性能车辆进行评估。这些轨迹源自作者最近提出的扰动感知最小圈时框架，其中最坏情况扰动增长在有限视界内传播，并用于收紧轮胎摩擦和赛道极限约束，在保持性能的同时提供概率安全裕度。LT和SE用作性能指标，而RMS横向偏差、速度误差和漂移角则表征驾驶风格。结果显示类似帕累托的LT-SE权衡：NOM产生最短LT但最高SE；TLC以更长LT为代价最小化SE；FLC位于效率前沿附近，相对于NOM显著降低SE而仅略微增加LT。移除轨迹引导（NOREF）会增加LT和SE，证实参考轨迹能提升速度和操控效率。总体而言，研究结果突显了基于参考和扰动感知的规划（尤其是FLC）作为训练工具和实现快速稳定轨迹的有效手段。

</details>


### [104] [Hybrid-Diffusion Models: Combining Open-loop Routines with Visuomotor Diffusion Policies](https://arxiv.org/abs/2512.04960)
*Jonne Van Haastregt,Bastian Orthmann,Michael C. Welle,Yuchong Zhang,Danica Kragic*

Main category: cs.RO

TL;DR: 混合扩散模型结合了开环控制例程和视觉运动扩散策略，通过遥操作增强原语（TAPs）在演示中引入预定义例程，使模型在推理时能自动触发这些精确控制例程，从而提高精度和速度。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统基于模仿学习的视觉运动策略虽然在复杂操作任务中表现良好，但在精度和速度方面仍不及传统控制方法。为了解决这一局限性，研究者希望结合开环控制例程的精确性和视觉运动策略的灵活性。

Method: 提出了混合扩散模型，开发了遥操作增强原语（TAPs）系统，允许操作员在演示过程中无缝执行预定义例程。模型学习在推理过程中自动触发这些TAPs，将开环例程与视觉运动扩散策略相结合。

Result: 在三个具有挑战性的真实世界任务上验证了方法：小瓶抽吸、开容器液体转移和容器拧开。实验结果表明该方法能够有效结合开环例程的精确性和视觉运动策略的灵活性。

Conclusion: 混合扩散模型成功地将开环控制例程与视觉运动扩散策略相结合，通过TAPs系统实现了在演示和推理过程中无缝集成预定义例程，提高了操作任务的精度和速度，为复杂机器人操作任务提供了新的解决方案。

Abstract: Despite the fact that visuomotor-based policies obtained via imitation learning demonstrate good performances in complex manipulation tasks, they usually struggle to achieve the same accuracy and speed as traditional control based methods. In this work, we introduce Hybrid-Diffusion models that combine open-loop routines with visuomotor diffusion policies. We develop Teleoperation Augmentation Primitives (TAPs) that allow the operator to perform predefined routines, such as locking specific axes, moving to perching waypoints, or triggering task-specific routines seamlessly during demonstrations. Our Hybrid-Diffusion method learns to trigger such TAPs during inference. We validate the method on challenging real-world tasks: Vial Aspiration, Open-Container Liquid Transfer, and container unscrewing. All experimental videos are available on the project's website: https://hybriddiffusion.github.io/

中文标题: 混合扩散模型：将开环例程与视觉运动扩散策略相结合

中文摘要: 尽管通过模仿学习获得的视觉运动策略在复杂操作任务中表现出良好性能，但它们通常难以达到与传统基于控制的方法相同的精度和速度。在这项工作中，我们引入了混合扩散模型，将开环例程与视觉运动扩散策略相结合。我们开发了遥操作增强原语（TAPs），允许操作员在演示过程中无缝执行预定义例程，例如锁定特定轴、移动到对接航点或触发特定任务例程。我们的混合扩散方法学习在推理过程中触发这些TAPs。我们在具有挑战性的真实世界任务上验证了该方法：小瓶抽吸、开容器液体转移和容器拧开。所有实验视频可在项目网站上查看：https://hybriddiffusion.github.io/

### [107] [Contact-Implicit Modeling and Simulation of a Snake Robot on Compliant and Granular Terrain](https://arxiv.org/abs/2512.05008)
*Haroon Hublikar*

TL;DR: 该论文提出了一个统一的建模与仿真框架，用于分析蛇形机器人在刚性、柔性和颗粒地形上的侧向蜿蜒和翻滚运动。采用接触隐式建模处理摩擦相互作用，结合连续介质和离散元方法模拟地形变形效应，建立了分层仿真流程。

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有机器人运动模型主要针对刚性地面，缺乏对柔性、颗粒等复杂地形中相互作用（如滑移、沉降、能量耗散）的准确建模能力，限制了机器人在非结构化环境中的可靠移动性分析。

Method: 1. 使用接触隐式公式建模分布式摩擦相互作用；2. 集成Project Chrono的土壤接触模型(SCM)模拟连续介质地形变形；3. 采用Chrono DEM引擎进行颗粒级离散元模拟；4. 通过MATLAB Simscape仿真和物理实验验证。

Result: 刚性地面模型能准确预测短期运动，而连续介质和颗粒级地形模型在软质和高度动态环境中对可靠移动性分析至关重要。仿真揭示了土壤破坏、间歇性脱离和能量耗散等刚性模型无法捕捉的机制。

Conclusion: 该工作建立了一个分层仿真流程，推进了在挑战性非结构化环境中操作的机器人的鲁棒、地形感知运动能力。不同精度模型适用于不同应用场景，实现了从实时控制仿真到高保真颗粒物理的完整覆盖。

Abstract: This thesis presents a unified modeling and simulation framework for analyzing sidewinding and tumbling locomotion of the COBRA snake robot across rigid, compliant, and granular terrains. A contact-implicit formulation is used to model distributed frictional interactions during sidewinding, and validated through MATLAB Simscape simulations and physical experiments on rigid ground and loose sand. To capture terrain deformation effects, Project Chrono's Soil Contact Model (SCM) is integrated with the articulated multibody dynamics, enabling prediction of slip, sinkage, and load redistribution that reduce stride efficiency on deformable substrates. For high-energy rolling locomotion on steep slopes, the Chrono DEM Engine is used to simulate particle-resolved granular interactions, revealing soil failure, intermittent lift-off, and energy dissipation mechanisms not captured by rigid models. Together, these methods span real-time control-oriented simulation and high-fidelity granular physics. Results demonstrate that rigid-ground models provide accurate short-horizon motion prediction, while continuum and particle-based terrain modeling becomes necessary for reliable mobility analysis in soft and highly dynamic environments. This work establishes a hierarchical simulation pipeline that advances robust, terrain-aware locomotion for robots operating in challenging unstructured settings.

中文标题: 蛇形机器人在柔性和颗粒地形上的接触隐式建模与仿真

中文摘要: 本论文提出了一个统一的建模与仿真框架，用于分析COBRA蛇形机器人在刚性、柔性和颗粒地形上的侧向蜿蜒和翻滚运动。采用接触隐式公式对侧向蜿蜒过程中的分布式摩擦相互作用进行建模，并通过MATLAB Simscape仿真和物理实验在刚性地面和松散沙地上进行验证。为捕捉地形变形效应，将Project Chrono的土壤接触模型(SCM)与关节多体动力学集成，能够预测在可变形基底上降低步幅效率的滑移、沉降和载荷重新分布。对于陡坡上的高能量滚动运动，使用Chrono DEM引擎模拟颗粒级粒度相互作用，揭示了刚性模型无法捕捉的土壤破坏、间歇性脱离和能量耗散机制。这些方法共同涵盖了实时控制导向仿真和高保真颗粒物理。结果表明，刚性地面模型能提供准确的短期运动预测，而连续介质和基于颗粒的地形建模在软质和高度动态环境中对可靠的移动性分析变得必要。这项工作建立了一个分层仿真流程，推进了在挑战性非结构化环境中操作的机器人的鲁棒、地形感知运动能力。

</details>


### [108] [From Generated Human Videos to Physically Plausible Robot Trajectories](https://arxiv.org/abs/2512.05094)
*James Ni,Zekai Wang,Wei Lin,Amir Bar,Yann LeCun,Trevor Darrell,Jitendra Malik,Roei Herzig*

Main category: cs.RO

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种从生成的人类视频到物理可行的机器人轨迹的两阶段方法，通过将视频像素提升为4D人体表示并重定向到人形机器人形态，然后使用物理感知的强化学习策略来模仿生成视频中的人类动作。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 视频生成模型在合成新情境下的人类动作方面进步迅速，有潜力作为上下文机器人控制的高层规划器。但关键问题是如何让人形机器人零样本地执行生成视频中的人类动作，因为生成视频通常存在噪声和形态扭曲，使得直接模仿比真实视频更困难。

Method: 提出两阶段流水线：1) 将视频像素提升为4D人体表示，然后重定向到人形机器人形态；2) 提出GenMimic——一个基于3D关键点条件的物理感知强化学习策略，使用对称正则化和关键点加权跟踪奖励进行训练。

Result: 创建了GenMimicBench合成人体运动数据集，使用两种视频生成模型生成多种动作和情境。实验表明在模拟中优于强基线，并在Unitree G1人形机器人上实现了连贯、物理稳定的运动跟踪，无需微调。

Conclusion: 这项工作为实现视频生成模型作为机器人控制高层策略的潜力提供了一条有希望的路径，能够从噪声生成视频中模仿人类动作，并在真实机器人上实现物理稳定的运动。

Abstract: Video generation models are rapidly improving in their ability to synthesize human actions in novel contexts, holding the potential to serve as high-level planners for contextual robot control. To realize this potential, a key research question remains open: how can a humanoid execute the human actions from generated videos in a zero-shot manner? This challenge arises because generated videos are often noisy and exhibit morphological distortions that make direct imitation difficult compared to real video. To address this, we introduce a two-stage pipeline. First, we lift video pixels into a 4D human representation and then retarget to the humanoid morphology. Second, we propose GenMimic-a physics-aware reinforcement learning policy conditioned on 3D keypoints, and trained with symmetry regularization and keypoint-weighted tracking rewards. As a result, GenMimic can mimic human actions from noisy, generated videos. We curate GenMimicBench, a synthetic human-motion dataset generated using two video generation models across a spectrum of actions and contexts, establishing a benchmark for assessing zero-shot generalization and policy robustness. Extensive experiments demonstrate improvements over strong baselines in simulation and confirm coherent, physically stable motion tracking on a Unitree G1 humanoid robot without fine-tuning. This work offers a promising path to realizing the potential of video generation models as high-level policies for robot control.

中文标题: 从生成的人类视频到物理可行的机器人轨迹

中文摘要: 视频生成模型在合成新情境下的人类动作方面正在快速改进，有潜力作为上下文机器人控制的高层规划器。为了实现这一潜力，一个关键的研究问题仍然存在：人形机器人如何以零样本方式执行生成视频中的人类动作？这一挑战源于生成视频通常存在噪声并表现出形态扭曲，使得直接模仿比真实视频更困难。为了解决这个问题，我们引入了一个两阶段流水线。首先，我们将视频像素提升为4D人体表示，然后重定向到人形机器人形态。其次，我们提出了GenMimic——一个基于3D关键点条件的物理感知强化学习策略，使用对称正则化和关键点加权跟踪奖励进行训练。因此，GenMimic可以从噪声生成视频中模仿人类动作。我们策划了GenMimicBench，这是一个使用两种视频生成模型在多种动作和情境下生成的合成人体运动数据集，建立了一个评估零样本泛化和策略鲁棒性的基准。大量实验表明在模拟中优于强基线，并确认在Unitree G1人形机器人上实现了连贯、物理稳定的运动跟踪，无需微调。这项工作为实现视频生成模型作为机器人控制高层策略的潜力提供了一条有希望的路径。

### [109] [STARE-VLA: Progressive Stage-Aware Reinforcement for Fine-Tuning Vision-Language-Action Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2512.05107)
*Feng Xu,Guangyao Zhai,Xin Kong,Tingzhong Fu,Daniel F. N. Gordon,Xueli An,Benjamin Busam*

Main category: cs.RO

TL;DR: STARE-VLA提出了一种渐进式阶段感知强化学习方法，通过将长时程动作轨迹分解为语义阶段，提供密集、可解释的阶段对齐强化信号，显著提升了视觉-语言-动作模型的微调效果。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有方法将长时程动作视为语言序列，采用轨迹级优化方法（如TPO或PPO），导致信用分配粗糙和训练不稳定。与语言不同，动作轨迹通过因果链阶段进展，各阶段学习难度不同，因此需要渐进式阶段优化。

Method: 提出STARE模块，将长时程动作轨迹分解为语义阶段，提供密集、可解释的阶段对齐强化信号。将其集成到TPO和PPO中，形成STA-TPO（离线阶段偏好优化）和STA-PPO（在线阶段内交互）。基于监督微调初始化，提出Imitation -> Preference -> Interaction (IPI)序列微调流程。

Result: 在SimplerEnv和ManiSkill3上的实验显示显著提升，在SimplerEnv上达到98.0%的成功率，在ManiSkill3任务上达到96.4%的成功率，实现了最先进的性能。

Conclusion: STARE-VLA通过渐进式阶段感知强化学习，有效解决了长时程动作轨迹优化中的信用分配问题，显著提升了VLA模型的动作准确性，为机器人操作任务提供了更稳定高效的微调方法。

Abstract: Recent advances in Vision-Language-Action (VLA) models, powered by large language models and reinforcement learning-based fine-tuning, have shown remarkable progress in robotic manipulation. Existing methods often treat long-horizon actions as linguistic sequences and apply trajectory-level optimization methods such as Trajectory-wise Preference Optimization (TPO) or Proximal Policy Optimization (PPO), leading to coarse credit assignment and unstable training. However, unlike language, where a unified semantic meaning is preserved despite flexible sentence order, action trajectories progress through causally chained stages with different learning difficulties. This motivates progressive stage optimization. Thereby, we present Stage-Aware Reinforcement (STARE), a module that decomposes a long-horizon action trajectory into semantically meaningful stages and provides dense, interpretable, and stage-aligned reinforcement signals. Integrating STARE into TPO and PPO, we yield Stage-Aware TPO (STA-TPO) and Stage-Aware PPO (STA-PPO) for offline stage-wise preference and online intra-stage interaction, respectively. Further building on supervised fine-tuning as initialization, we propose the Imitation -> Preference -> Interaction (IPI), a serial fine-tuning pipeline for improving action accuracy in VLA models. Experiments on SimplerEnv and ManiSkill3 demonstrate substantial gains, achieving state-of-the-art success rates of 98.0 percent on SimplerEnv and 96.4 percent on ManiSkill3 tasks.

中文标题: STARE-VLA：面向视觉-语言-动作模型微调的渐进式阶段感知强化学习

中文摘要: 近期基于大语言模型和强化学习微调的视觉-语言-动作（VLA）模型在机器人操作方面取得了显著进展。现有方法通常将长时程动作视为语言序列，并应用轨迹级优化方法如轨迹偏好优化（TPO）或近端策略优化（PPO），导致信用分配粗糙和训练不稳定。然而，与语言不同，动作轨迹通过因果链阶段进展，各阶段学习难度不同，这促使了渐进式阶段优化。为此，我们提出了阶段感知强化（STARE）模块，将长时程动作轨迹分解为语义阶段，并提供密集、可解释、阶段对齐的强化信号。将STARE集成到TPO和PPO中，我们分别得到了用于离线阶段偏好优化的STA-TPO和用于在线阶段内交互的STA-PPO。进一步基于监督微调作为初始化，我们提出了模仿->偏好->交互（IPI）序列微调流程，用于提高VLA模型的动作准确性。在SimplerEnv和ManiSkill3上的实验显示出显著提升，在SimplerEnv上达到98.0%的成功率，在ManiSkill3任务上达到96.4%的成功率，实现了最先进的性能。

</details>

### [110] [Towards predicting binaural audio quality in listeners with normal and impaired hearing](https://arxiv.org/abs/2512.04792)
*Thomas Biberger,Stephan D. Ewert*

Main category: eess.AS

TL;DR: 该研究扩展了eMoBi-Q音频质量模型，通过加入非线性听觉滤波器组来考虑听力损失对音频质量感知的影响，特别是将响度作为预测正常听力和听力受损人群音频质量的子维度。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的eMoBi-Q音频质量模型虽然有效，但未考虑听力损失对音频质量感知的影响。听力受损者普遍存在响度感知改变的问题，因此需要扩展模型以包含响度作为音频质量的子维度，从而更好地预测听力受损人群的音频质量体验。

Method: 研究扩展了eMoBi-Q模型，加入了非线性听觉滤波器组。滤波器组参数及后续处理阶段基于Pieper等人（2018）提出的生理学基础（双耳）响度模型。目标是整合响度作为预测正常听力和听力受损人群音频质量的子维度。

Result: 研究提出了扩展的双耳质量模型的初步实现，该模型能够考虑听力损失对音频质量感知的影响，特别是通过整合响度作为重要的子维度。

Conclusion: 该研究成功扩展了eMoBi-Q模型以考虑听力损失的影响，初步实现了整合响度作为音频质量子维度的双耳质量模型，为预测听力受损人群的音频质量提供了重要基础。

Abstract: Eurich et al. (2024) recently introduced the computationally efficient monaural and binaural audio quality model (eMoBi-Q). This model integrates both monaural and binaural auditory features and has been validated across six audio datasets encompassing quality ratings for music and speech, processed via algorithms commonly employed in modern hearing devices (e.g., acoustic transparency, feedback cancellation, and binaural beamforming) or presented via loudspeakers. In the current study, we expand eMoBi-Q to account for perceptual effects of sensorineural hearing loss (HL) on audio quality. For this, the model was extended by a nonlinear auditory filterbank. Given that altered loudness perception is a prevalent issue among listeners with hearing impairment, our goal is to incorporate loudness as a sub-dimension for predicting audio quality in both normal-hearing and hearing-impaired populations. While predicting loudness itself is important in the context of loudness-based hearing aid fitting, loudness as audio quality sub-measure may be helpful for the selection of reliable auditory features in hearing impaired listeners. The parameters of the filterbank and subsequent processing stages were informed by the physiologically-based (binaural) loudness model proposed by Pieper et al. (2018). This study presents and discusses the initial implementation of the extended binaural quality model.

中文标题: 预测正常听力和听力受损听众的双耳音频质量

中文摘要: Eurich等人（2024）最近引入了计算效率高的单耳和双耳音频质量模型（eMoBi-Q）。该模型整合了单耳和双耳听觉特征，并在六个音频数据集上进行了验证，涵盖了通过现代听力设备常用算法（如声学透明度、反馈消除和双耳波束成形）处理或通过扬声器呈现的音乐和语音的质量评分。在当前研究中，我们扩展了eMoBi-Q以考虑感音神经性听力损失（HL）对音频质量的感知影响。为此，模型通过非线性听觉滤波器组进行了扩展。鉴于改变的响度感知是听力受损听众中的普遍问题，我们的目标是将响度作为预测正常听力和听力受损人群音频质量的子维度。虽然预测响度本身在基于响度的助听器拟合背景下很重要，但响度作为音频质量的子测量可能有助于为听力受损听众选择可靠的听觉特征。滤波器组和后续处理阶段的参数基于Pieper等人（2018）提出的生理学基础（双耳）响度模型。本研究介绍并讨论了扩展的双耳质量模型的初步实现。
